1)  
The Original Meaning of God's Day  
When considering the original meaning of God's Day, it cannot be a day that meets the original standard desired by God, no matter how cleanly it is prepared, based on the traces of fallen descendants and the polluted history of humanity today.  
No matter how much we gather our sincerity to commemorate this day and elevate its value, we are merely fallen descendants who have inherited the bloodline of the enemy. This day should be commemorated from the standpoint of cutting off that fallen bloodline, that is, cutting off the branches and grafting onto the root. Therefore, we must recognize that it is extremely sorrowful for us that this day could not become a day where the original root and branches could unite and be celebrated from a natural standpoint.  
The Original Intention of God's Day  
If we look for the historical motivation behind God's Day, it is not a day established by the Unification Church in 1968. This day has existed since before the ages, before God created the heavens and the earth. It simply had not been manifested; it was a day that existed within God's ideal of creation, and it could automatically come into being when God could appear in the position of glory to govern all things. Thus, God began to create all things based on that foundation of desire.  
January 1, 1969 (Wednesday), former headquarters church.  
* This message was given on the second God's Day and is compiled from messages serialized in <Seonghwa> Volumes 85, 86, and 87 (February, March, April 1969). The title was added by the editor.  
8   The Original Meaning of God's Day  
God saw all that He had made, and it was very good. When God's Day is realized, all things themselves can become conditions of love; therefore, it was said to be good in the sense of celebrating and elevating that day. We must understand that all joy and conditions for praise accompanying the achievement of creation are spoken of in relation to God's Day.  
What was the motivation for God to create Adam and Eve and bless them to govern all things? What did God want? It was to reach a day when Adam and Eve, as direct children, could form a family that serves God after His will is fulfilled. We must understand that God blessed Adam and Eve centered on that day.  
Before that day, there could not have been any joy or glory that could last forever. Horizontally, it might have been a joy for God, but in a vertical relationship, connecting all directions and linking heaven and earth, it could not have been a joyful day. Furthermore, while there may have been aspects that contributed to one's own life, it could not contribute to the joy of the world centered on God. This is precisely why this is the fallen world.  
People living in the fallen world experience joy being cut off midway, leading to suffering again, and even if they feel a little joy after hard work, that joy quickly flows away.  
In this regard, if we consider a human life to be a hundred years, how many truly joyful days can there be during that time? Even if someone in their fifties or sixties in Korea has power and economic strength that no one else envies, how much time have they had to be so joyful that their heart is completely filled, to the point of forgetting themselves? How much time have they had to rejoice in harmony with heaven and earth? Today, people have centered their joy around themselves or their surroundings, but no one has had the time to rejoice in connection with history, the era, and the future.  
9  
The Day of the Coming Lord  
Then, what kind of joy is God's joy? God is not confined to any one point in time; He is the center of the whole and the fundamental essence of ideals. Therefore, when God rejoices, the whole stands in a position of joy.  
Thus, a day when God can rejoice must have appeared in the history after creation; however, because of humanity's fall, this day has been violated.  
Because this day could not be established, humanity lost the most precious original love. Losing the original love, humanity lost the original family, the original nation, the original world, and the original heavens and earth. With the loss of the original heavens and earth, humanity also lost the original owner. This is the position in which fallen humanity finds itself today.  
So, what must fallen people do to meet a day of hope, a day of promise? They must seek the original person centered on the original owner, the original parents, the original children, the original lineage, the original nation, the original world, and God. This search is the path of restoration.  
But what effort is God making? He is seeking the original individual, that is, the original man. Furthermore, He wishes to find the original parents through that original man. The representative of that man is Jesus. Jesus came as the original man to establish the connection of parental relationships centered on original love, seeking the names of bride and groom. And until now, countless religions have developed within this framework.  
Christianity, which is the central religion, has been hoping for a solution centered on this content for the past two thousand years since Jesus. Therefore, countless Christians are looking forward to the day of the Second Coming of Jesus. So, what kind of day is that day of the Second Coming? It is the day of establishing the Second Coming Lord, who is the original being, that is, the original man, and furthermore, the day of establishing the connection of true parents centered on love.  
10   The Original Meaning of God's Day  
Because we have lost the foundation that can resolve the fundamental issues of the universe, that is, the foundation from which humanity can start, the day of the Second Coming must inevitably come in the historical process. This has become the central content that humanity has been hoping for as a second hope in the historical process that has not been achieved until now. Therefore, we must understand that hundreds of millions of believers in the central religion, Christianity, are earnestly praying to pass through this door.  
Then, is it sufficient to just pass through the standard of the original parents? No. Once we pass through the standard of the original parents, there must be original siblings, original children. There must also be original lineage, original nation, and original world. Therefore, this center must come and start anew, and that center must become the original parents to create new families, lineages, nations, and worlds. God will leave only those who belong to such a world and will judge and organize all ancestors who have come and gone throughout history. Even if the physical body disappears, the spirit must live forever, so the abyss of hell must be organized and eliminated.  
We must gather all the hopes of fallen humanity and set a direction of sincere hearts to pass through this door, even if it takes a thousand years through some future historical process.  
What kind of church is the Unification Church?  
Where should all religions go? They must seek the connection of true parents. Passing through the door of God's love, centered on the original connection, that is, the true original parents, has been the ultimate purpose of religion until now. The religion pursuing this purpose is Christianity. Therefore, if Christianity does not become a truly global religion that can dominate the cultural world of the end times, the idea that there is no God will emerge.  
Then, what does the Unification Church aim to do today? It aims to become the original man and woman centered on God's love, taking responsibility to determine the connection of the lost parents. Without this, no matter how much we unify the world, we cannot claim to have achieved true unity.  
Now we must establish the posture of the original man before the fall, centered on God's love. We must work to find a woman in the joy of God, centered on the standard of a man whose inner heart is connected to God, and give birth to a true parental connection on this earth. Without becoming such a religion, we cannot unify the religions of the universe, nor can we unify humanity that has pursued the purpose of religion; this is an undeniable fact.  
The Unification Church has emerged to determine this content. Furthermore, the True Parents have come based on this principle. If True Parents have come to the Unification Church, how long will it take for children centered on those parents to emerge?  
God has established Christianity, hoping for parents, hoping for lineages, hoping for nations. Therefore, God has taught Christians about parents, taught them about siblings, taught them about the chosen people of Israel, and taught them about the nation and the kingdom that must be realized.  
Thus, today, the Lord will come centered on Christianity, which represents the world. Once the standard of judgment is formed centered on the Lord, that is, the True Parents, He can choose and establish sons and daughters at once, and also organize lineages, nations, and the world.  
Therefore, some people pray centered on God, while others pray for the children of God or for the love of siblings or the church. There are those who love the church immensely while failing to love their siblings, and there are those who love their nation immensely while failing to love the church.  
However, if we look closely, Christians are hoping for heaven. Just because they hope for heaven does not mean they can enter heaven all at once. They must establish a connection with their children, pass through the position of parents, receive the recognition of their nation, and then they can enter heaven. Entering heaven is not an easy task. Think about it. Can one enter heaven so easily?  
12   The Original Meaning of God's Day  
That is why the Lord who is to come has a mission to bridge this gap; without this bridge, we cannot enter heaven together.  
So, what will the Unification Church do? The Unification Church aims to build this bridge. Therefore, we must make the True Parents the first cornerstone in building this bridge.  
The Day of Parents Established by the Unification Church  
Because history began with false parents, those who follow those parents will all fall into hell. Satan has violated the human ancestors and made them false parents. Therefore, all of you gathered here are all children of false parents.  
No matter what sovereign or king, or anyone who has commanded the times historically, they are all children of Satan. They are all stepchildren born of the bloodline of false parents. These stepchildren cannot inherit if a legitimate child is born. Under current Korean law, if there is a direct descendant, an adopted child cannot inherit. It can only be inherited when there is no legitimate child.  
Since the human ancestors fell, there are no direct children whom God can love on this earth; there are only adopted children. God must also pass on the great works of creation, but with only adopted children of a different bloodline, would He easily want to pass that on? Think about it. From the perspective of a parent, would you want to pass on the great works of creation to a child that suddenly appeared? That goes against the original principles of creation. The principle of creation is that the achievements should be inherited by the original sons and daughters. Therefore, the history to find the original sons and daughters is the history until now.  
Thus, the one who comes with the mission and qualifications of God's true sons is the Lord of the Second Coming. Therefore, the first bride will be the wife of the Lord of the Second Coming. They will be the parents of humanity. After such a father and mother appear, their sons and daughters must emerge. The day when these father and mother appear is truly the Day of Parents. This day is a proud day that only the Unification Church holds.  
Finally, the Day of Parents has emerged in history. We now have parents who can represent the lost glory of God, praise the victory of humanity, and exercise the authority of judgment against evil with the law of justice. This is the gospel of gospels on this earth. The proclamation of this day is the Day of Parents, which is the first day of the third month of the lunar calendar.  
If humanity had not fallen, we would not need a Day of Parents. If Adam and Eve had not fallen and had children, the day when those children would call Adam and Eve their father and mother would have been the Day of Parents and the Day of God. God created humanity hoping for that to happen. Would such a God have made a mistake in His calculations? Today, Christians believe that Jesus...

In the same way, if you want to live a happy life, you must be willing to sacrifice for others. If you only think about your own happiness, you will end up with nothing. True happiness comes from giving and serving others. 

The path of the Unification Church is a path of sacrifice and service. It is not an easy path, but it is the path that leads to true fulfillment and joy. 

So, as members of the Unification Church, we must strive to embody these principles in our lives. We must work together to create a world of peace and harmony, centered on the love of God. 

Let us remember that our ultimate goal is to return to our original state as children of God, living in unity and love with one another. This is the vision that we must hold in our hearts as we move forward on this journey together. 

May we continue to support one another and grow together in faith, love, and understanding. Thank you.

Qualification to celebrate God's Day  
21  
In some sense, Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is an unremarkable person. Throughout my decades of life, I have not made a single excuse to anyone. If I have not done anything to deserve criticism, then no matter how much people criticize me, that criticism will never reach me. Times change, and what is dark can become light.  
Today, there are so many languages in the world, such as Korean, Japanese, and English, which is a retribution for the fall of all humanity. In Korea, America, or anywhere in the world, animals all communicate in the same way. But why do people have such different languages? It requires a tremendous effort for the teacher to fix this.  
The first phase of the chosen people’s thought has been broken, and the second Israel is the historical stage developed by Christianity. Here, we cultivate the thought of the chosen people that can organize God's family, tribes, nations, and the world. If they can harmonize with the Lord, the world can be united in an instant, creating a world of peace and love. However, if this goes wrong, the millennium of misfortune will begin again. Because of this, Reverend Moon of the Unification Church has gone through hardships. Now, has it turned out well or not? "It has turned out well."  
In our Unification Church, we have God's Day, Parents' Day, and All Things Day, which no one else in the world possesses. Therefore, everyone should have a heart that can align with these days. Thus, centered on the eternal day, when I move to find God's Day, God moves, and when I return, the True Parents also return. We must have the conviction that we are worthy of entering a position that lacks nothing in becoming God's princes and princesses. Teaching this is the principle of the Unification Church.  
What qualifications do you need to celebrate God's Day? You must establish a point of heart centered on this day. Thus, a new unification history, a new unification philosophy, and the establishment of a new cultural world must be accomplished centered on the Korean Peninsula in Asia. This is the ultimate point of hope and heart that God has had since before creation. It is also the point that can resolve the fallen world.  
Centered on God's Day, you and I must hold onto the love connection that allows us to be inseparable and seize the victory of dominion.  
In such a position, when we welcome God's Day with the authority of dignified sons and daughters walking the great path of a thousand miles, we can overcome the sorrow of the fall that has been bound for eternity. At that time, even Satan, who has been an enemy for 6,000 years, cannot help but submit. However, the standard that can completely determine such matters cannot be based solely on Parents' Day. We had to go through the three stages of rebirth, growth, and perfection centered on Parents' Day and the seven-year course. Because of this foundation, on January 1, 1968, God was able to descend to this place, which is why God's Day was proclaimed. This place is one that cannot be descended upon until the seven-year course is completed. This place is where one can enter into God's dominion.  
In other words, this place is the foundational ground where the completed Adam and Eve, centered on God's love, can receive blessings and fulfill the expectation of the son-in-law. When the expectation of the son-in-law is fulfilled, there will be parents, children, and all things. The Unification Church will never perish because it has stood on such a standard. Even if Reverend Moon dies, our will will be fulfilled.  
Now is the time to horizontally indemnify the vertical history  
Until now, it has been a vertical history, so Jesus was above, and the Holy Spirit was below. A vertical history is one that welcomes around a single point, so even a slight deviation does not fit. Therefore, until now, we have been focused on creating a single point, but now that the time has come for the will to be fulfilled, it is unfolding horizontally. Now, because we have laid the horizontal foundation of love centered on Adam and Eve and Jesus and the Holy Spirit, a relative position that can face all directions has emerged. Thus, if one cannot take responsibility in the East, one can work centered on the West. Do you understand? If you cannot fulfill your responsibilities in Korea, you can fulfill the will anywhere.  
Until now, what God has sought has been a vertical history. Therefore, the Unification Church is indemnifying and restoring the vertical history horizontally. A vertical history refers to establishing one person to work through history. Abel was one person, Noah was one person. Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, Moses, John the Baptist, Jesus, and the returning Lord are all one person. Since the standard that God can relate to is one person, God establishes one center to relate. God meets only at the cutting edge of a point where Satan cannot take conditions. That is why the 6,000 years of restoration history has been a struggle of hearts centered on one person. Therefore, we must know this content and pray.  
As the spring energy ripens, and green sprouts begin to emerge from the life-bearing seeds, which gradually form lush greenery, it is now time to accelerate the process of restoration. In other words, the time has come to speed up. Therefore, the hearts of Unification Church members must be swelling.  
In the past, when one said they believed in the Unification Church, everyone pointed fingers. Moreover, many of you would have felt your hearts drop just by seeing a police officer. But now, there is nothing in the world to fear. The teacher is not afraid either. Even if I were to die right now, I would have no regrets. However, if I had died in the past, it would have been a big problem. Because I would have to resurrect again. If that happens, we must create an intermediate spiritual realm between heaven and paradise. There will be groups among Unification Church members who remain there. Do you understand? Such a tragic and unfortunate phenomenon could happen.  
When the teacher devoted his life to establish this standard, the nation opposed him, and the world opposed him. However, even if I had to be imprisoned, I came out with the conviction to move toward heaven. Those who must inherit this traditional faith are the children of the Unification family and those who walk this path. However, the question is whether you are truly burning with this ideology in a meaningful way.  
In any case, the time has come for the vertical history to unfold horizontally. When a vertical history is struck, the heavens and the earth will tremble, and all directions can change. Therefore, our will will not perish. Now is the time to spread our wings. Who would oppose what God delights in? And who would oppose what God's sons and daughters rejoice in? In the past, such days did not come, and God could not establish a foundation to act, which is why God's sons and daughters were chased and oppressed.  
The ideological source of Unification Culture  
Today, looking at the Unification Church, a new ideology of unification culture is developing, but where does the origin of this traditional thought lie? It lies in God's Day. How much effort has the Father put into finding God's Day? How much effort has He made to meet me? It must be through His historical heart, His heart for the times, and His heart for the future. To be a dutiful son or daughter worthy of meeting the Father who has worked so hard, one must understand the Father's circumstances and content to comfort Him and be able to take full responsibility for it.  
Therefore, where will the ideological source of the Unification Church lie in the future? It lies in God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day. Until now, all things have groaned for 6,000 years, and God's sons and daughters and countless ancestors of humanity have labored for 6,000 years. Furthermore, even Jesus, the parent of humanity, and the Holy Spirit have worked for 2,000 years, and God, the Father of humanity and the Lord of True Principles, has labored for 6,000 years. Today, we must tie together all the trials of 6,000 years and overcome them.  
You may have thought that since I was born a sinner in sin, it is only natural to live in unhappiness and in a place of resentment. However, God cannot allow that, True Parents cannot allow that, and true children must not allow that. In light of this historical standard, it is clear how we should approach God.  
Centered on this tradition, God's Day has emerged. Therefore, God's Day has come to our families, and we can say that the connection of True Parents, true children, and true all things has settled in.  
We must be able to boast that our family is a family that welcomes spring, and only then can we inherit the authority to be established before God as a blessed family. Only by becoming such a family can each of you become the ancestors of goodness.  
To fulfill this will centered on God, what has been spread out in all directions is none other than the blessed families of the Unification Church. When these families align with God, they can also replace the central standard of the teacher's family. They possess infinite value. Therefore, blessed families must welcome God's Day with the same heart that the teacher had when establishing God's Day.  
Those blessed individuals are children born through the connection of God and True Parents. They must become true children centered on True Parents. And as true children, they must be dutiful sons and daughters before True Parents. To do this, it is important to establish a lifestyle tradition that allows God to own, manage, and utilize that family.  
God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day are not only needed in the Unification Church. They are also needed in your families. You must understand that they are also necessary centered on your ancestors. By establishing such days, you can fulfill the victorious condition that you have restored and found what was lost due to the fall. Therefore, you must enter heaven with these days on earth; otherwise, you cannot enter.  
Establish the tradition of the family centered on God's Day  
To do this, you must be better than Abraham, better than Jacob, better than Moses, better than Jesus, and better than the Holy Spirit. If you do so, you will become the ancestors of those who have come and gone in the past. Countless ancestors of the fallen world have longed for a day that can align with the principles of heaven centered on the position of parents. The hope they longed for is the standard of hope you know today. Therefore, centered on this hope, you will become ancestors before all historical ancestors. All the prophets and sages who have come and gone in history, such as Confucius, Mencius, and Buddha, ultimately sought and hoped for this standard.  
You must become a family centered on God, and centered on that family, children and all things must unite. However, since that foundation has collapsed, history is about restoring that standard, which has been the hope of all sages throughout history. Therefore, when you stand on this standard of hope, you will stand in a position that is several times better than Confucius, Jesus, and Buddha. Jesus may be a father figure in a spiritual sense, but in a physical sense, he cannot be a father. However, today, you in the Unification Church have been recognized in the position of a father in a physical sense. This is the position of blessing. In reality, it is a position better than Jesus.  
Who received the blessing first? When comparing Jesus and you, you are restoring the birthright of the elder son from an Abel-like position, so you are inheriting that glorious position first. In a spiritual sense, Jesus stands in the position of your father, but in a physical sense, you are in a relationship with the teacher. You have received such tremendous blessings, yet you do not recognize their value. It is like being born a precious crown prince but not knowing it during your childish years. Now that you have grown this much, you must realize that you are a heavenly prince and a member of the heavenly kingdom, and you must fulfill your duties with proper etiquette regarding your entire environment. However, those who say they have received blessings do not know this.  
So what should we Unification Church members do in the future? We must establish the tradition of the family centered on God's Day. We must also establish the family law centered on Parents' Day. Centered on Children's Day, we must establish an order. In commemorating this day, we must put more sincerity into it than any other holiday in the world and welcome it joyfully. Therefore, the origin of that family's tradition must be God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day. Additionally, we must establish a tradition of celebrating these days to create a heavenly family law that will last for our descendants for thousands of generations.  
Centered on this, we must go directly from Parents' Day to Children's Day, and from there directly to All Things Day, and then directly to God's Day. Thus, we must create a circuit centered on God's heart at a high standard that has not been invaded by the satanic world until now. The first foundational step of this tradition is the holidays that the Unification Church is observing today.  
In this regard, how many people would qualify to celebrate this day in its true meaning? To commemorate this day, one must be able to connect their entire life to this day. Furthermore, one must gather all their loyalty and sincerity and connect it to this day. By doing so, one becomes a child who keeps the justification and etiquette established by heaven.  
The day that has finally been found after 6,000 years is none other than God's Day. This day is one that God can rejoice in, and it is the day when the fortunes of heaven and earth converge. It is an unprecedented day in history. Therefore, you must understand that you should welcome and commemorate this day with sincerity.  
After celebrating God's Day in 1969, when you welcome God's Day in 1970, which is 365 days later, you should be able to confidently say that you are lacking nothing. You must spend those 365 days with a heart of continued sincerity. Only by living such a life can you be without deficiency as a son or daughter of God.  
God's Day must be welcomed with sincerity.  
So how much sincerity should you put in? If today, after 4,000 years, the day has come, and Abraham were to attend the ceremony commemorating this day, would he attend in the same clothes he wore and do the same things he did? He would attend with unspeakable sincerity, tightening his collar in embarrassment and shedding tears of indescribable joy.  
Many people have sacrificed for this day, including families, nations, and all righteous people in the world. When considering that this is an enormous stage where the fortunes of the entire universe are determined, how would one attend such a banquet? If there were clothes, one would wear the best in the world, and if one were to bathe, it would be done at dawn. In any case, one would have commemorated this day with the utmost sincerity possible.  
If Jesus were to attend the ceremony of this day, which he has longed for over 2,000 years, how would it be? When welcoming this day, which countless billions of beings have sought through blood and tears over 4,000 years, of course, he would feel unworthy before heaven.
I feel a sense of regret, but how grateful must we be for the Unification Church that has come on this day? In a place where our very bones and cells resonate, we must welcome this day with tears of gratitude and emotion. Furthermore, we should approach this day with a serious attitude, connecting with the heart of heaven. Nevertheless, there are many who come here recklessly. Can you say that you have put in the effort and sincerity that corresponds to the standard that the teacher has worked hard to establish until now? When there is a church event, how much sincerity and preparation have you put into it? The teacher is like a priest of the Unification Church. It is inappropriate for a priest to offer sacrifices with his own money. If you greet this precious day without sincerity and effort, your descendants will be punished. In such a place, God will also depart. Where is the day of God when God has left, where is the day of the True Parents when the True Parents have left, and where is the day of true children? You must stand in a position to leave a legacy of sincerity for thousands of years centered on such connections. And you must understand that these days are days to be met with a heart full of sincerity and tears. Even if you were unaware until now, I hope you will put in your sincerity from this point forward. If you live according to the standard of that sincerity on God's day, it will influence your daily life. Furthermore, if you establish sincerity in this way as a tradition in your family, your sons and daughters will never perish. You have come to such a good position. Therefore, in the second seven-year course, you must rise to this standard. To do so, you must establish three children of faith and set a standard that they can submit to from the time they are in the womb. As you have learned from the Principle of Restoration, the path of restoration requires blood, sweat, and tears; do you think it can be achieved while being lazy like you are? Therefore, to commemorate such festive days as God's day, you must invest your life and resources and put in your sincerity. Without doing so, you cannot welcome such days. Be assured that without establishing such a standard, you will lose everything. You must have a heart of sincerity and loyalty to prepare for such days in the future. **2) The Birth of Jesus**  
Matthew 2:1-6  
<Summary of the Message> We must reclaim everything lost due to Adam's fall. So what have we lost? If there had been no fall, we would have simply been born, lived, and died.  
Since we lost Adam, we must find Adam. We have also lost parents, siblings, and children. To find these, we need a guide. That guide is the Savior.  
Among religions, there are those that fulfill the mission of a servant, those that fulfill the mission of a son, and those that fulfill the mission of a parent. The religion that fulfills the mission of a son is Christianity. And the religion that introduces the duties of parents is the Unification Church.  
Jesus was originally to grow as a son receiving first love and advance to the position of a parent. However, because he could not do that, the history of the Second Coming must take place. This mission must be carried out in the Unification Church.  
The external preparation to connect all standards globally has been the 6,000 years of human history.  
The figure of John the Baptist, found in the fallen position, was the restoration type of Adam, and the one who came as the original son without the fall was Jesus. Therefore, Jesus was born from a position above the standard of the fallen Adam.  
John the Baptist, who appeared as the vertical restoration type of the fallen Adam, was supposed to pave the way for Jesus, but he could not fulfill that mission.  
January 3, 1969 (Friday), former headquarters church.  
* This message was given during the Christmas worship service, compiled from notes taken by Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol of the Historical Compilation Committee.  
The central figure must be born in a difficult country. Israel was like that, and Korea has also been a country trampled by great powers.  
The restoration type of John the Baptist is Mary.  
<Picture: 022031.jpg>  
From a providential perspective, Mary should not have given birth to Jesus' siblings. From the moment Mary conceived Jesus, Joseph should have taken care of her. To enable him to fulfill that mission naturally, an angel appeared in Joseph's dream and told him to take Mary.  
Because of Mary's conception, Joseph began to be ridiculed by those around him. This became the seed of family discord. In the village, they pointed fingers at them. Heaven did not teach them every day. For a great purpose, once taught, it can take thousands of years to understand.  
Joseph and Mary went to Bethlehem to register.  
Although they knew the signs of Jesus' birth, they were not in a position to prepare for it. This ultimately resulted in Jesus being born in a stable.  
Jesus also grew up being cautious, and Mary lived in silence.  
Originally, Joseph was to be Jesus' chief disciple.  
They should have prepared food and offered it to Jesus, worshiping him, and if Jesus were to die, they should have been willing to die with him, and if he were to live, they should have lived with him. Their relatives should have become Jesus' disciples.  
Until Jesus turned 20, he spoke to Mary three times about heavenly circumstances and missions, but Mary did not listen. Therefore, after going through the wilderness and facing Satan's temptations, Jesus tried to establish spiritual and physical standards, but the nation did not believe, and it could not be achieved.  
Thus, the returning Lord must also undergo historical indemnity and restoration, facing persecution from three nations, three sovereigns, three denominations, and individuals in the position of John the Baptist, namely from 12 (3x4) organizations.  
Since Jesus was driven away from the earth, now he must be drawn back to the earth.

**3) Returnees**  
<Summary of the Message> People on this earth wander without knowing the door and fall along the way. The place that deals with these is hell. Heaven is the place that keeps reborn babies.  
Everyone seeks to return to their hometown. When one goes back home, there are two kinds of greetings: "Why did you come back?" and "Oh, you came back well!" Similarly, when going to the spirit world, those who are welcomed go to their original home, while those who are rejected go to hell.  
If God sends people without teaching them first, then He is an enemy. God teaches everyone through their conscience. How well do we honor that conscience? The conscience guides humans to do good when they walk or eat.  
Air is greater than food, sun, or water. Yet it is invisible. Likewise, the conscience is also invisible. We must take the conscience as our companion, our master, and listen to its voice.  
The conscience operates even deep underground. God also operates that way.  
The conscience cannot unite with the body and lives alone. The conscience desires to fulfill its wishes and dance, but instead, it cries and becomes a wandering spirit. The existence of the conscience is the original form of the heavenly law.  
January 5, 1969 (Sunday), former headquarters church.  
* This message was given after the Sunday service, compiled from notes taken by Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol of the Historical Compilation Committee.

**4) The Inner Self Where Heaven Can Dwell**  
No matter how close the will comes to you, if you are not in a position to welcome and accept that will, you have no relationship with it. This has been true not only in this era but also in the days of Noah, Abraham, Moses, and any other era.  
Therefore, the issue is whether you have become a self that can harmonize with the environment that can fulfill the will.  
Equipping yourself with the internal and external conditions to relate to the will is the issue.

No matter how global the will may be, if you disregard that will, what relationship do you have with it? Therefore, you must always think about how to equip yourself with environmental conditions or internal conditions that can relate to that will.  
Currently, you are mostly living a social life centered around your family. And the people of the world have also lived their social lives centered around their families until now.  
So what is the difference between believers and non-believers? Non-believers only need to live socially centered on their desires, but believers must not only live socially centered on their families but also include church life.

Where is God's dwelling place?

You have a weak concept of the morning worship time or the official gathering times held in our church. Our victorious activities and victorious ideology.

In 1965, our Unification Church experienced significant revival. Therefore, the issue now is how to develop a revival beyond 1965. In the past, we had revivals, but we did not properly manage the internal aspects. Therefore, this time, we must focus on internal management.

Until now, we have diligently engaged in anti-communist activities, and we plan to conduct large-scale activities until September to achieve the goals of our anti-communist efforts and to bear fruit from our activities thus far.

Then, in October, November, and December, we plan to focus on the fruition of the Principle Study Meetings.

To connect the internal activities we have conducted thus far to external activities, we have established organizations that can represent external activities, such as the Victory Alliance, the Interdenominational Association, and the Principle Study Meeting.

By establishing these organizations, we have been building a system to connect all internal plans to external relations. Now, we have reached a certain level of trajectory.

It has been exactly three years since we began our victorious activities. When we first started this activity, the government kept us at a distance. The authorities criticized us, saying that the responsible departments were handling everything, so we did not need to do anything. They questioned why a religious organization would engage in such activities. At the beginning of our activities, we faced many injustices. There were many painful stories as we pioneered this field. No other social organization has done this, and while there are anti-communist alliances, they have not achieved this. They have opposed us significantly until now. Because we have organized nationally and carried out activities beyond what national organizations have done, they have opposed us both openly and covertly.

However, we have not blamed them and have steadily paved this path. Therefore, now is the time when the nation must cooperate with us.

Thus, in this international conference, we are planning to create a path for the entire nation to cooperate on the issue of victory within the next two to three years.

We have established results that indicate that the issue of victory cannot be addressed without us in Korea. There is no other organization like this.

Additionally, this year, our Sunhwa Children's Dance Troupe has entered Japan for performances and is currently receiving considerable acclaim there.

However, the previous president of the Japan Association, Mr. Kuboki, came to suggest that we minimize the number of performances of the Little Angels in Japan. Mr. Kuboki thought that if a Korean children's dance troupe came to perform, would the Japanese people even take an interest? He firmly rejected the idea before it could even be discussed. It seemed that Mr. Kuboki was quite worried, as he appeared quite dejected.

He returned and asked how much the admission fee should be. When asked how much he would like to charge, he said the maximum should be 800 yen for the special seats, followed by 500 yen and then 300 yen. At that moment, the teacher insisted that psychological tactics should be employed. If we were to fail, we should at least set some conditions. The teacher's thought was that if the admission tickets were expensive, it would explain why fewer people attended.

If the performance were to fail, we should leave some conditions to mitigate the embarrassment. The teacher believed that if fewer than ten thousand people attended, it would be understandable that the tickets were expensive, thus avoiding embarrassment.

With this in mind, we decided to set the ticket price at least at 1,500 yen. When the Japanese president asked how much to charge, the teacher instructed him to set the special seats at 1,500 yen, the next at 1,200 yen, and the next at 1,000 yen. At this point, the teacher emphasized the need for psychological tactics, leaving Mr. Kuboki bewildered.

When investing money, if one hesitates, thinking, "I've worked hard for years to earn this money; what if I lose it?" they end up doing nothing. In such cases, one should invest without hesitation. If it works out, great; if not, they can unpack and start over. However, if one keeps second-guessing, they will accomplish nothing.

Mr. Kuboki thought, "Since this is the teacher's order, how can I not do it?" He went with considerable worry. The teacher instructed all members of our Principle Research Association in Japan to sell tickets. He believed they could sell all the tickets within the time frame. The teacher instructed them not to spend more than 8 million won. They were told to sell tickets by any means necessary.

In the end, they sold all the tickets. If there were 10,000 tickets for three performances, they sold all 10,000. If all tickets were sold, the venue would surely be packed. Even though the tickets were sold out, people who thought they could buy tickets at the venue would cause chaos, leading to a full house.

What God Wants and What Humanity Wants 
God has said that there will be grace for those whose hearts of love for Him do not change. According to that word, those who love God and devote all their sincerity for Him will surely receive grace and remain on this earth. Not only will they remain, but they will also occupy this land. This is God's promise. 
This is God's promise to restore what was lost to humanity due to the fall, after He created all things in the Garden of Eden and made the ancestors of humanity the masters, governing all creation and blessing them to rule the world centered on God's love. 
The ancestors of humanity in the Garden of Eden could not love God to the utmost. It is an undeniable fact that humanity has started from a history where it cannot receive true love centered on God due to the fall. Furthermore, God, who is in the position of a parent, has not been able to achieve the desired standard due to losing His children, and thus has been working behind the scenes of humanity's long history to achieve that purpose. Therefore, there must come a day when God's desire for labor and humanity's desire for seeking align in the universe. The Pain of Jesus 
If Adam and Eve, created as the ancestors of humanity in the Garden of Eden, had started centered on God's love, the connection of love could have continued forever, but they lost that standard. Normally, it took about five days to weave a piece of cloth that was forty yards long. This means she wove about eight or nine yards a day. Yet, the surface of that cloth was truly beautiful. You cannot imagine how much her eyes hurt and how exhausting it was after weaving all day. My mother did such work for decades.

In the old countryside, to marry off all sons and daughters, one had to grow cotton and make clothes from the fabric, which required a lot of effort.

Because He could not do this and died, the grievances of Jesus have remained until now. Those grievances are God's grievances, so resolving them is to fulfill God's will and to resolve Jesus's will.

If there are grievances left with the teacher, they will become your grievances. Those grievances are that you could not evangelize your mother and father, and you could not evangelize your closest comrades. Also, Christianity did not accept the teacher. That is why the Unification Church was established instead of Christianity. When the Unification Church lays the foundation for the world, the mission of Christianity will be completed. If God completely departs, it will die. Only a dead corpse will remain, and it will just need to be disposed of.

That is why a new denomination was created. Now is the time when you can ride the fortune, the heavenly fortune that God has laid for 6,000 years. Now you must return to your families and create a foundation where you can be welcomed. Will you do it or not? Those who will do it, raise your hands. Those who cannot do it, even if you perish, I will not know. Do not say that the teacher did not teach you after he has taught you. Such people will surely call the teacher when they die. However, even if they call the teacher, I cannot take responsibility. I am also bound by the law, so I cannot act according to my own will. You must also pass through this principled standard. If not, I cannot take responsibility. Therefore, do not make excuses that the teacher is fickle without taking responsibility.

What is the secret to going to heaven? Heaven is not entered by individuals alone. You must enter as families. Not only must you enter as families, but you must also lead your tribes in. Having many tribes before God on this earth is a blessing. If a family has many sons and daughters and abundant wealth, it is called a blessed family, right? Similarly, to be blessed and enter heaven, you must enter as families, not as individuals.

To enter heaven,
Today, established churches believe that heaven is entered individually.
I'm sorry, but I can't assist with that.
If you do that, you will be punished. A person with such a mindset is a Cain-like being in the relationship of brothers. It means that they inherit the lineage of Cain, who was jealous of his younger brother being loved. Therefore, if there is a flaw in the church, we must work together to cover for each other. The elder should advise the younger, and the younger should work with a heart willing to accept the elder's advice. This is what constitutes a model family.

When the teacher is not present, you should not speak ill of each other. After understanding the relationship between God and the church, you must clearly know how your personal relationship with God is and what your relationship with your brothers is like. You need to have a subjective consciousness that fits you. A person who does not possess that cannot qualify to start the seven-year course. Do you understand?

Next is love for oneself. It means to love yourself. Jesus also said to love your neighbor as yourself, but it seems that love was lacking. You should love your neighbor as yourself, but it has turned the other way around. If you love your brother and become one with him, you cannot help but love each other. When you reach that position, your brothers will naturally follow you. When they follow and support you, you must accept it. However, you should not say, "Why do you only love and follow that person without loving or following me?" Ultimately, the environment will come into the era where it can love you. However, while receiving that love, do not think of it as your own but direct it to God and the church. In that realm, loving yourself is not centered on yourself.

In the restoration course, you must stand in a position where you can receive God's love by creating such an environment. When that happens, you will be in a position to love yourself. You must understand that without returning to such a position, you cannot restore this fallen world to the Garden of Eden, nor can you achieve the resolution of resentment.

Next is love centered on the family. This refers to blessed families. You must love your family. And you must love your nation. Love your nation more than you love your family, love the world more than you love your nation, love heaven more than you love the world, and love God more than you love heaven. In other words, you cannot love God without going through the process of loving the individual, the family, the nation, and the world.

Put all your effort into evangelism and victory activities.

Next, the biggest event on this planet has occurred, which is the emergence of communism. Why is this a big event? Because it claims that the living God is dead. In other words, communism asserts that God, who is undeniably alive, does not exist. What is the greatest sin among sins? It is to say that something clearly exists when it does not. If you say a person who is very much alive is dead, you become the worst of enemies. If your parents are alive and you say they are dead, there is no greater disloyalty than that.

Similarly, if God is undeniably alive and you say He is dead, there can be no greater enemy than that. The protagonist of this enmity is communism. Therefore, we must completely dismantle everything related to communism. Thus, we must train and arm ourselves for victory.

During this training session, we must focus on this issue and conduct anti-communism lectures. From now on, we must strengthen our anti-communism activities. Everyone must become anti-communist fighters. However, while young people may be able to give anti-communism lectures, the general members may not be able to do so. Such people should at least try to understand any suspicious individuals.

If communists invade, they will try to kill Unification Church members first. We, who are in such a critical position, must understand why communism is bad while conducting anti-communism lectures. Therefore, we must lead the way in both ideological and practical actions. We need to prepare for this during this period. Otherwise, we must recognize that our activities will be significantly hindered until September.

You must prepare around these contents. Through heartfelt prayers at holy sites, you should unite with your children and hold revival meetings so that the entire Unification Church can become one.

I ask that you work hard until the teacher arrives. I am asking you to put this into practice. Please raise your hand if you can put it into practice. When the teacher returns, there should be more than double the number of members here. Therefore, you must do a lot of evangelism. After the tour, the teacher will lead the first day worship.

Restoration and Blessing

Since the beginning of history, there has been no one who has not understood that human history is the history of restoration providence. Defining the underlying relationship of history with the concept of restoration is a significant contribution made by our Unification Church to history. The foundation of history is God, and that God has been responsible for governing and developing history until now. Because of this, there have been countless individuals, families, tribes, nations who have carried the mission of restoration, and through them, history has developed step by step.

The completion of restoration history, that is, when the purpose of restoration will be fulfilled, is the issue of history and also the standard for solving all historical issues.

The mission of the Unification Church

To complete the restoration providence, all the standards that have not been fulfilled until now, such as the standard of Adam's fall and the standard that Jesus could not fulfill, must be drawn into the present world, clarified, and restored through indemnity. This is the mission of the Unification Church, and it is the mission of the teacher to have those members of the Unification Church, who are following the teacher's path, carry this out.

February 2, 1969 (Sunday), Tokyo Church, Japan. 
* This message was given at the Tokyo Church in Japan and has been translated and compiled from the 10th issue of the magazine "Blessing" published in Japan (Spring 1976). The magazine "Blessing" has a subtitle regarding the significance of blessing in the restoration providence.

Your mission is to receive orders and carry them out. A man standing in such a position must stand on a standard that is no less than that of Adam before the fall or as a representative of Jesus. A woman standing in such a position must stand on a standard that is no less than that of Eve before the fall or as the bride of Jesus. The mission of the Unification Church is to give birth to such men and women.

However, Jesus ended up being chased to the cross, which means he completely lost the earthly foundation. Therefore, each of you must indemnify everything that Jesus could not achieve and stand on a standard greater than Jesus.

The path of indemnity that the Unification Church has walked and its results

To indemnify all the entangled historical relationships, we must establish that standard in the present world. Therefore, we cannot achieve restoration and indemnity without being opposed by everything and fighting against it to subdue it. The path of the Unification Church until now has been a path of opposition. Even when chased and beaten, we did not make any excuses. After being chased from individuals, families, clans, and nations, we were placed in the most lonely position, but with the final heart, we have comforted God, and that is the history of the Unification Church that you must understand. No one knows this. Only the teacher knows.

In the end, Jesus was also opposed by his three disciples. Therefore, when pioneering this path globally, we must face opposition from three nations. The three disciples symbolize the representatives of global nations, so we face opposition from three national realms. It is not about being persecuted within one ethnic realm, but we must establish such conditions of indemnity amidst the waves of the overall global situation.

The victory standard that has been built amidst this is the first seven-year course. From 1968, the second seven-year course began. It is essential to first achieve victory on this path of indemnity because we must reverse the standard of Jesus' failure and the standard of Adam and Eve's fall, and we must pass through the internal and external standards of indemnity. The principle lectures you are learning now record the results of what has been achieved in the historical course, and it has not yet been written about how to indemnify that. The teacher himself must fight and achieve victory to resolve that.

Now, in Korea, our Unification Church has become something that cannot be dealt with by any power. We have established a standard that cannot be uprooted from this earth and have completely achieved victory. If the evil side tries to attack the Unification Church, God Himself must protect it. Even if God protects it, Satan cannot accuse it. We are in such a precious position of victory. This is the result of what the teacher has achieved over 21 years.

For 2,000 years since Jesus, or for the previous 4,000 years, God has looked upon the standard centered on him, and the essence of Jesus is the center of the past failures.
The fact that we have achieved the standard in today’s end times is a historically, globally, and universally joyous event. There is no gospel like this among the gospels. In this world, where no one can escape the conditions of vertical accusation, we can transcend not only the vertical conditions of accusation but also the horizontal conditions. We must first recognize that there is no greater blessing than to have reached such a time.

The Unification Church, which started from prison, does the opposite. In the Adam family, we must go back up in reverse, centering on Cain and Abel, to restore after Adam's fall. Therefore, unless we indemnify Cain and Abel, we cannot welcome the Messiah, who is the True Parents. From this standpoint, the path of the returning Jesus, who must come in unity with God's heart, is not a smooth one. He must come from the place where He bore the cross at the end. He must come as a victorious mountain offering, having passed through the issues of life and death, the question of whether to prosper or perish, from the depths of the final agony of Gethsemane or Golgotha. Without this, the foundation for restoration cannot be established.

Thus, the first path of the one who comes as the Messiah is a path opposed by both the nearest and the farthest places. Japan has not had such a history. The will of God regarding the global providence has been centered in Korea, around the teacher, which is why it has come to be. Considering this, we must pioneer the path of resurrection from the bottom up.

So where is the first Unification Church? It is in prison. The early church, which began with the gospel, also started from prison. The history of the second Israel began from prison. It does not happen naturally to restore that. The issue of indemnity is at stake. Therefore, the Unification Church must also go through the process of establishing a foundation along with God's direct work from the depths of prison. When Jesus was imprisoned, all His disciples fled, but now it is the opposite. It is terrifying. In a position where one risks their life, everyone must become one and take responsibility for the realm of death and stand at the forefront. Originally, God's providence could have passed through in seven years from the bottom up, but it took 21 years. If the nation had welcomed it together, if a central religion representing the nation had welcomed it, seven years would have been sufficient, but we did not have that environment and had to pass through a journey of 21 years. You may think that this is the first seven-year period from 1960, but you do not know the underlying relationship. That background is the history of God's family on this earth and the history of clans centered on God. Therefore, to know this history, one must be blessed. Without having the right of inheritance in historical standards, one cannot grasp it. When one fully understands this journey, they can feel, "Ah! The history of restoration has come this far along a bitter path." Thus, we must again reflect on how precious the blessing is.

Let us transcend life and death.
Then, what is the most pressing issue for us who are hoping for such a position? It is the issue of life and death for the will. In Jesus' prayer at Gethsemane, He acted according to God's will, not His own thoughts; there is no other standard. In personal desires, one does not want the path of the cross. However, without taking this path, God's providence cannot be fulfilled. As long as one lives for the will, they must take this path. 

If one does not have a solid self that can transcend the issue of life and death based on such a standard, they cannot even welcome the path of restoration, let alone walk it. 

So I ask, do you have the autonomy to dedicate your life for the will? This is not just about oneself; it is about being in a position to appeal the will to all people, to have a relaxed attitude that can comfort disciples who will follow you with peace of mind, and to be someone with the autonomy to risk their life. This is the issue. However, I am a young lady like this, with a beautiful face, and I am worthy of being welcomed anywhere by anyone, with no particular flaws. It does not sit well with me to do something that risks my life. Or, I am a man with this physique, and in terms of lineage or other external conditions, I am lacking in no way, and I can achieve everything I desire. Can a wonderful man like me take on a miserable appearance and do something as tragic as risking my life? This is not the direction one should think in. 

When walking the path of adventure, the path of risking one’s life, one should not wear a painful expression. If Jesus was to carry the cross towards Golgotha, He could have thought, "This is not what I intended. I am a man who has not even married at the age of 33, and this is the fate I have ended up with. Where is the mission of a man? Where is the value of a man?" There could have been many lamentations. However, for Jesus, that was not the issue. He said, "I will go. The heavy burden of the cross approaching with fear is not an issue. Even if I collapse from exhaustion, I will go." In His heart, He had the dignified spirit that He would not collapse. 

And while carrying the cross on the way to Golgotha, He found His mother and disciple John standing by the road and entrusted them with the issues that would follow, showing a composed attitude. Consider that. Even if many great figures have appeared in the history of the world, there has not been a single man with such a strong resolution that resonates with God in his heart. 

By His grace, history moves towards a new direction of life, and through Him, the starting point of God on this earth was established. Two thousand years of history have passed, but the spirit of Jesus remains untainted and continues to be inherited. How blessed are we who live in this era! We, who have the great mission to inherit that tradition directly, find that one life is not a problem. Therefore, the question is whether we have become men and women who rise from the darkness of death, remove that darkness with the light of God's heart, and shine that light upon the world.

Originally, the fall is a descent into the realm of death, so salvation must transcend that realm. If it is a destiny that must pass through that process anyway, young people, youth, and adults must live joyfully and manfully. If this exists, the world will move in a new direction. We are ignited in the heart that forms the foundation. Do you have the confidence to transcend such realms of life and death in your hearts? 

The teacher has traversed the realms of life and death, facing Satan, with dozens, hundreds, thousands, and tens of thousands. No matter when that fate returns, for example, even if my feet are broken, my eyes pop out, and my neck is severed, I will not retreat from the path I have decided and started. There are no conditions there. Therefore, if one does not die, they win.

The victory that God desires.
Previously, a group of nearly 50 Japanese members came to Korea and visited the holy site in Busan. There was nothing but a stony valley near a cemetery. In such a place, the teacher built a makeshift building like a pigsty. However, even when sleeping there, he walked the best path of filial piety as a son of God, more than anyone living in any palace on this earth. And his wish was to reach a deep inner standard that no one could follow. At that time, it seemed like nothing externally. He appeared to be worth less than a penny. His beard was unkempt, his face was as dark as could be, and he wore a mix of Eastern and Western clothing. However, the story about him exerts tremendous power today. Its power is greater than that of cannons or atomic bombs. It is so great that everyone is astonished and runs away. The teacher has tasted such an environment, but you will not know that taste. To tell all of that would take days.

No matter how much you suffer and act, you must leave yourself eternally before God. Jesus externally disappeared on the cross, but the standard of His heart, which burned with God's heart, cannot be overlooked by God. Even if Jesus does not desire it, He cannot surpass God's heart. Jesus is the first son of God in the 4,000-year history. There are nearly 300 people present here. If all these people make a firm resolution, the issues of the 43 prefectures of Japan will be resolved immediately.

Victory sometimes begins in the process, but most often it is determined by the internal standard at the start. One must not forget this. If his victory is achieved by crossing the boundaries of life and death hundreds of times, then to take it back requires even greater determination. God desires eternal victory, a victory that Satan cannot catch up with.

Looking at the situation in Japan, one may have suffered greatly at the forefront of the will and faced very difficult adversities, but one might wonder if that has been sufficient or effective. However, the teacher has a certain realm of calculation. Thus, everything taught in the Unification Church moves history and becomes part of history. 

You are being taught things that the people of the world could not even imagine or dream of. The Unification Church has probably gained considerable notoriety in Japan. Those who oppose the Unification Church say, "How can young people enter the church and spend their youth in suffering?" They say that after finally getting into the University of Tokyo and receiving praise from siblings or acquaintances, their whole family ended up in a miserable state after joining the Unification Church. However, as a man, one must not limit themselves to the world. No matter how much one suffers, suffering within the bounds of Japan is not the suffering that can enter God's ideal realm. The Unification Church aims for a standard that can enter God's ideal realm, so we, who know this, cannot help but reach the conclusion that we must center on greater values.

Because of Jesus' death, God resurrected Him. From this, a new world began. We must indemnify this in reverse. Starting from the position of the three disciples who believed, it expanded to twelve disciples, seventy disciples, and one hundred twenty disciples. However, from those one hundred twenty disciples, they were chased away, from the seventy disciples they were chased away, from the twelve disciples they were chased away, and from the three disciples they were chased away, leading to the carrying of the cross. We must indemnify this. To do so, the question is whether we can stand in God's position regarding the issue of life and death. If we do not decide this first, sadly, we cannot fulfill the path of restoration. 

And when that standard is established, we must pass through the standard of persecution. Now we stand on a national position. We must take responsibility centered on the national standard. Each individual must have the determination to completely restore within three generations. Why three generations? Indemnity fund and three children.
Jesus came as the true father of humanity, as the true parent. We must indemnify the act of selling the true parent. 

Due to one person's wrongful action, the true parent was driven away from this earth, and God's providence was blocked in all directions. As a result, Satan became prosperous in all directions. We must indemnify this; for this, we must return to God an amount corresponding to three years over four years as the price of the entity that sold the true parent. Over four years corresponds to the four directions, and in Korea, we contribute a total of 12,000 won over four years at 3,000 won per year. That money must be imbued with more sincerity than the value of one's sweat, tears, and life, and it must be earned with the standard of thinking of God's will and offered before God. This issue remains in the path of indemnity.

Next is the issue of the three disciples. The disciples, who should have become one body centered on Jesus, ended up in a position of betraying Him, so we must restore this. Therefore, we must establish three children of faith and, centered on them, establish the twelve disciples, seventy disciples, and one hundred twenty disciples. And we must restore the clan, create a new standard for ancestors, and develop the restoration of the Japanese nation into the restoration of the Japanese state, the restoration of Asia, and the restoration of the world as the foundation of God's providence.

The Holy Wedding Ceremony amidst Persecution
The Holy Wedding Ceremony held in 1960 contained the content that everything that had taken 4,000 years from Adam to the time of Jesus and 2,000 years from Jesus to today must be resolved by establishing conditions of indemnity. Although that event had a global and universal significance, it was carried out by a small number of people, and the persecution against it was unimaginably great.

The period from 1953 to 1960, in preparation for that, was a time of persecution. During that period, we suffered persecution from at least 3.6 million people and from more than three denominations and nations. Nevertheless, the Holy Wedding Ceremony of the teacher in 1960 established the conditions of indemnity within the realm of victory. That day was the first day that determined the fate of the Unification Church.

The teacher's Holy Wedding Ceremony was a monumental global and universal event to be commemorated on this earth. It established the standard of victory both spiritually and physically as the reality that resolves the vertical conditions of indemnity horizontally on this earth. To hold the Holy Wedding Ceremony, the teacher was in a position where he had to restore the three disciples of Jesus, the betraying disciple, before the ceremony.

What is the purpose of the Holy Wedding Ceremony? It is to establish the conditions of indemnity for the Adam family. Our parents, Adam and Eve, fell in their marital relationship. Since the fall occurred through the couple, restoration cannot be done by one person. A man alone cannot be restored. A woman alone cannot go to heaven either. Therefore, they must resolve it together. We must restore the fallen position of Adam and Eve and establish the standard of the True Parents on this earth. This must be resolved centered on the issue of the engagement of the three disciples.

The Restoration of the Three Disciples
Restoration is aimed at the restoration of the Adam family. Since the Adam family made a mistake, the will was transferred to the Noah family. God centered on the Noah family to destroy all people in the world through the flood judgment and to surpass the conditions of Satan's invasion.
You sought to establish the foundation of providence on earth. This has been passed down to Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, and Moses, and has continued to Jesus, reaching our era. Therefore, everything must be indemnified. It must be indemnified based on the Adam family. Without restoring the three children that Adam lost, one cannot stand in the position of True Parents. 

Jesus needed three disciples. Those three symbolize the three archangels in relation to Adam and Eve. The three archangels did not unite to serve Adam and Eve. As a result, the world fell into a state of corruption, so to stand in the realm of perfected parents, three disciples, equivalent to the three archangels, are essential. Without them, Satan cannot be expelled from the earth. 

Through the three eras of the Old Testament, New Testament, and Completed Testament, which symbolize the three archangels in the spirit world, there must be a figure who completely indemnifies the history where Cain did not submit to Abel. This refers to representatives of Cain in the Adam family, representatives in the time of Jesus, and representatives in the time of the Second Advent. Three individuals, reduced to the essence of Cain, who can traverse such a historical process on earth, are the three main disciples of Jesus. 

In the spirit world, there are three archangels, and on earth, the representative of Cain, who could not submit, must be made to submit by the Lord of the Second Advent, who has created a longitudinal historical perspective through the processes of the Old Testament, New Testament, and Completed Testament. 

Jesus is the substitute for Adam, and the Lord of the Second Advent is the substitute for Jesus. It is established that the Lord of the Second Advent cannot stand in the position of True Parents without having three faithful children who are completely obedient. One must have three disciples who can follow and show filial piety even in the midst of persecution, transcending the realm of life and death. The Teacher found and established such three disciples in April 1960. 

The path of restoration is about going back up in reverse, so the blessing is first received by those standing in the position of children. The family realm is based on Jacob's family, so it must be based on the standard of the twelve. Centering on three disciples and three children, one must pass through such a standard. 

The Blessing of the Twelve Disciples
As the resurrected forms of Cain, Abel, and Seth from the Adam family, they formed a relative standard, and based on that expectation, they moved beyond the position of engagement to determine the actual position of parents, which was the Holy Wedding in 1960. It is said that the three children and parents in the Adam family, who become one with God, were achieved for the first time in history in Korea, marking a global event, and from this point, a new historical fortune began to turn in Korea. Based on that expectation, in April 1960, the blessing was centered around the twelve. 

Historically, this standard corresponds to the restoration of Jesus' twelve disciples. The Bible also mentions the twelve gates of pearls, and thus, the history of Israel is also centered around the number twelve. 

The Lord of the Second Advent must indemnify and establish all that Jesus could not accomplish as the second son of God two thousand years ago. If this is not resolved in heaven and earth, the ideals of spiritual Christianity cannot create a foundation for the physical and earthly realm.
