When God becomes the overall motive and accomplishes things, then indemnity follows. The reason there are still not many members in the unified world is the responsibility of the headquarters. 

The headquarters gives, while the counterpart receives. Heaven knows the purpose of providence, but the earth generally does not know and follows. God, who knows this, has created an environment in which humans can move. The headquarters must also pioneer the history of creation in this way. We must be sent for the world and strive for the environment. 

From 1968 onward, the era will change. We must act spiritually and materially. This is not just a church with a few people gathered; it is the headquarters of the world. 

We must continue to separate. Then we will replace the position of the teacher. 

If the entire membership of Korea does not restore Korea, we cannot restore the world. However, Heaven is preparing the environment for the next stage of restoration. 

Korea must go to the world. 

We must carry out the movement to offer for God materially. 

We must work for three days in each season, totaling twelve days a year, and offer it to God. 

May 4, 1969, (Sun), Former Headquarters Church. 
* This message was given after the dawn worship and was recorded by Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol of the Historical Compilation Committee in his notebook. The title was added by the editor. 

The headquarters must give. Receiving first and then giving is merely repaying a debt, not giving. The position of the owner is to say that they have eaten without eating themselves. It is good to plant and then harvest, but trying to harvest without planting is the mindset of a thief. There should not be more receiving than giving. Practicing before praying is more precious than praying. 

You must go abroad to become a proactive patriot. Those who are not externally equipped must be even more sincere. If you give sincerely but the counterpart does not stand on the standard, the blessing will return. One should not take for granted what is received from a high position. Regret not being able to give. It is like a parent who holds back what they want to eat and gives it to their child. 

Practice before praying. 

Give and quickly forget. It will be kept in Heaven. 

Japan must receive blessings first, which is why Kubo Ki was called in during the 436 couples' blessing. 

From June to September, anti-communist activities must be carried out. 

Now, pray for the country (Korea). 

Evangelize one person each month. If you evangelize one person a month to a death row inmate, can it not be done? We are also in a natural death penalty situation where we will die in a few decades. 

On that day, the principle will accuse. 

Blessed families that cannot have faithful children will receive severe accusations. It is strange to know the formula and not act on it, eating and sleeping instead. There is nothing more frightening than teaching the formula and saying not to evangelize. 

Put in three times the effort and sincerity into raising worldly sons and daughters. Otherwise, restoration will not happen. 

You must fulfill your family responsibilities. 
If you regard the work of building heaven as a neighbor's business, heaven will also be a neighbor's business. 

<Jesus and Us> 
<Prayer> Father! May Your children across the nation gather at this time to worship before You, and may You be present with them. Also, may Your glory dwell in every place where Your sons and daughters scattered around the world look towards this place and worship You. 

We have returned here after completing the long journey of the world tour according to Your will. We thank You for listening to the heartfelt prayers of many members and protecting us during this time. As our hearts that have longed for You meet again, we are in a position where we must speak of Your story and pledge to fulfill our responsibilities at this time, so we earnestly hope that You will personally preside over us. 

May no one else preside over this time and place, but may You personally preside over it. From now on, may all the time we dedicate be in accordance with Your wishes, and may it become an opportunity for us to devote ourselves to Your will. 

Father, please accept this Sunday worship, which we offer for the first time after returning to Korea, as holy. May You directly preside over it, and may only the results of the will You are orchestrating appear in this place. I earnestly ask for this. 

May 4, 1969, (Sun), Former Headquarters Church. 
* This message was given on the first Sunday after returning from the second world tour. 
<Seonghwa> It has also been serialized in Issue 87 (May 1969), Issue 88 (June 1969), and Issue 89 (July 1969). 

Thanks to your sincere efforts and prayers, I have returned safely. Today is the first Sunday after returning, so I hope everyone is filled with grace within the realm of the words allowed. And for those who are here for the first time, it seems that today will take a long time, so I ask for your patience even if it feels tedious. 

At this time, I will not report on everything that has happened in the world just because the teacher has returned from the world tour. Rather, we must now have a new resolution centered on our purpose, so I will speak about the overall content centered on our purpose. 

Until now, countless Christians around the world have believed in Jesus and sought the path of salvation, but among them, many do not have a clear understanding of the mission Jesus had when He came to this earth and the path He had to take. Furthermore, there is ambiguity regarding the highest purpose for which God sent Jesus to this earth. Therefore, at this time, I will speak under the title of "Jesus and Us." 

Jesus came to resolve God's overall providence. 
We members understand well that the providence of salvation is indeed the providence of restoration. Restoration means returning. To return, we must return to a position that surpasses the standard before the fall of humanity's ancestors, Adam and Eve, in the Garden of Eden. Our members know this well through the principle. 

When Jesus came to this earth, He had to reclaim everything that Adam lost due to his mistake. He was to establish one nation and one world. This was the overall mission of Jesus when He came to this earth. However, to reclaim that, He had to return. Returning is not simply going back without any content. It is essential to return through the opposite path of the fallen history. 

After 4,000 years of Adam's fall, Jesus was sent among the chosen nation of Israel, not for any personal mission, but to resolve the overall providence of restoration, that is, the content of God's overall providence. 

The life Jesus began when He came to this earth to preach the gospel was not for Himself but for the entire world. We must understand that it was a life that started to fulfill a mission on behalf of the overall history. Jesus, who labored for three years in the limited environment of Israel, was crucified after His efforts. 

From God's perspective, the fall of Adam and Eve was an unspeakably sorrowful fact. To restore this, God sent Jesus to this earth, but since Jesus could not fulfill His purpose and was crucified, this also became an unfathomable sorrow for God. 

Why did Jesus fail to fulfill His purpose? If we do not understand this clearly, the content of Jesus and our content will not be clarified, and the relationship between Jesus and us will also not be established. 

God established Mary and Joseph and sent Jesus to their family. After Mary conceived Jesus, she gave birth to Him under Joseph's protection. The Bible simply records that Jesus was conceived by the Holy Spirit. However, this is not a simple matter. For Jesus to come to this fallen world, He had to come from a position that was unrelated to original sin. 

But how did Jesus, born through Mary's womb, stand in a position unrelated to original sin? This is a problem that cannot be resolved theologically. Why? Because Mary herself is undoubtedly a descendant of fallen ancestors, and it is a fact that Jesus was born of Mary's blood and flesh. How then is Jesus without original sin? 

From this perspective, while we say that Jesus is without original sin, we do not know why He is without original sin. 

There are many religions on this earth, each with its own leaders. Some of these leaders have established their own purposes and have grown their religions into global religions. So, what is the difference between these religious leaders and Jesus? The issue of why everyone must believe in Jesus to be saved has not been clarified until now. 

Many religions on this earth claim that they will unite the world based on their own doctrines. So, from the believer's perspective, what is the difference between Christianity and other religions? What is the standard that can be said to be different? It is whether there is original sin or not. 

From a bloodline perspective, many religious leaders were also born as descendants of fallen ancestors, and it seems that Jesus was born in the same position. Of course, Jesus was conceived by the Holy Spirit, but it is undeniable that He was born through the womb of Mary, a descendant of the fall. So how can Jesus be without original sin? 

We know that when we are born on this earth, we are not born through loving, good parents whom God loves, and who live within God's will and serve that will. In other words, we were born through fallen parents. Therefore, according to Christian doctrine, we must be reborn. 

We were born, but we were born wrongly, so we must be reborn. To be reborn, it is not through the old parents but through new parents who are not those parents. 

We must be reborn through the True Parents to achieve complete salvation. 

So, what kind of parents are the new parents? The fallen Adam and Eve from the Garden of Eden were fallen parents, but the parents who must give birth to humanity again must be those who stand in a position that is not fallen, aligned with God's will, and can receive God's approval as the original parents. They must be parents who can establish an ideal family centered on God's love and can bear good children, standing on the original standard. Those parents are unrelated to the fall. 

Therefore, the necessity of being reborn does not mean being born again through the blood of fallen Adam and Eve's descendants, but rather being born again through the blood of parents who are unrelated to the fall. Without this, one cannot return to God. The root of sin began with Adam and Eve, so one must step over this and have the qualification of being born from a position unrelated to original sin to return to God's side. 

When viewed this way, what kind of savior does fallen humanity require? It must be a savior who can give birth to humanity from the position of true parents who are not fallen, standing in the same position as unfallen Adam and Eve, and who can receive God's love and blessings. Otherwise, humanity cannot rise to a position unrelated to original sin. 

What is the purpose of God wanting to save humanity? Under the realm of the fall, no matter how much one tries to save, salvation cannot be achieved. Therefore, God sent true parents who are above fallen Adam and Eve to this earth, and through those parents, humanity must go through the process of being reborn so that they will have no eternal relationship with Satan and that Satan will not be able to accuse them. Thus, only God can govern and intervene. 

In such a position, humanity cannot return to a place free from original sin without being reborn. 

What is the difference between Christianity and other religions? Other religions may teach about the savior, but the content regarding the savior is different. Among other religions, some come with the mission of being a servant before God, while others come with the mission of being adopted children before God. However, Christianity is different. It is based on the position of having sent the son of God to this earth to be the parent who can give birth to humanity again. 

Such a religion must be the last religion among religions, and it cannot be anything but the final religion that God has sent among the many religions on this earth. A religion that does not have such content cannot save the countless people of the world. From this perspective, Christianity stands in such a position. 

So, what is the purpose of Jesus coming to this earth? Before saving the nation and the world, Jesus Himself must stand in the position of parents who are not fallen, not in the position of fallen parents. Jesus must stand in that position. This is the difference.
Today, there are countless people on this earth, but all of humanity has descended from fallen ancestors, so they all stem from the root of original sin. No one has been born into this world through true parents who stand in a position free from the infringement of the fall. Not a single person has been born in such a way. How deeply do you feel that you were born from false parents?

If a person is sick, they must be healed. If a weak person becomes ill, they should not be healed to the same weak state they were in before. They must be restored to a state of health that exceeds that condition. Similarly, the fall signifies that humanity has broken down and fallen into the world of evil; therefore, we must repair what is broken and lift ourselves back up to the position before the fall in order to attain salvation. Salvation is essentially restoration. To restore, one must return not just to the old standard before the fall, but to a position that surpasses that standard. Thus, humanity, born through false parents who possess original sin, must be reborn through true parents who transcend original sin.

For this reason, there must be one individual who can stand in the position of true parents to give birth to all of humanity again. That person must not come to a position lower than the standard where Adam fell. They must come to a position above that. When viewed through the lens of principle, true parents must be born in a position that is absolutely unrelated to original sin, on a foundation that has undergone the process of indemnity. This is a concept that is unique to Christianity and is not found in general religions.

What is this about? It concerns Cain and Abel. Cain and Abel came out separately and fought as brothers. However, inversely, the younger brother must dominate the elder brother. You have learned about the theory of the fall and understand well that originally, because we humans fell, we were born with the blood of false parents. In other words, we were born with the lineage of Satan. You may not fully realize this fact, but whether you do or not will determine whether you can definitively resolve original sin in the future.

We were born with original sin through false parents. The Bible metaphorically states that Jesus is the true olive tree and we are the wild olive trees. What is the difference between the true olive tree and the wild olive tree? Their appearance is the same. However, their essence is different. So, how can the wild olive tree become a true olive tree? It must be grafted. It cannot simply be connected to the root. No matter how splendid and good its appearance may be, its fruit will have no relation to the true olive tree. Therefore, the wild olive tree must be cut off and grafted onto the true olive tree.

Why must it be grafted? Because humanity has fallen. The wild olive tree came to be because humanity fell. If humanity had not fallen, we would have become true olive trees. However, due to the fall, we became wild olive trees. If humanity had not fallen, there would have been no need for Jesus or religion.

The meaning of being grafted onto the true olive tree
The Bible states that one must be born again. The phrase "must be born again" implies that one was born incorrectly. When a person is born into this world, through what are they born? Are they born through the tree of the knowledge of good and evil? No. They are born through love. A person is born through the love of their parents. However, our ancestors were born through love, but they were not born through the joy of love that God could love and proclaim to the entire universe. They were born through a love that made God extremely sorrowful and that Satan greatly rejoiced in.

Humans are born through the love of their father and mother. However, because that love was flawed, being born from it means being born incorrectly. There is no way around it. Because we were born through this flawed love, we became wild olive trees, and therefore, we must completely cut off those branches and graft onto the true love branches of the true olive tree. We must completely cut off the branches of the wild olive tree that have grown for thousands of years and carefully graft them onto the true olive tree.

How can one be born again? Christians say that one must receive the baptism of fire through the Holy Spirit. So, what is this baptism of fire that one must receive in order to be born again? Today, Christians are told to believe without questioning, from one to ten, and from ten to a hundred, all in a muddled way. As a result, Christianity today is unable to relate to the advanced scientific civilization that continues to analyze and discover causes and effects, and it has failed to establish a close relationship with human life, leading to its gradual decline in the present world. Therefore, Christianity stands in a position of being criticized today.

What is the reason that humanity has been born incorrectly? It is because of flawed love. If love had not been flawed, humanity would have been well born. What is the fall? It is the act of having flawed love. In the Old Testament, to become God's people, one had to be circumcised. So, what is circumcision? Why does receiving circumcision make one a son or daughter of God and a member of God's people? This is based on the law of indemnity. When something is broken, the broken part must be repaired in order to be fixed. Otherwise, it cannot be repaired.

In the history of the Bible, the firstborn did not receive the blessing. Why did the firstborn not receive the blessing? Because it was predetermined that the firstborn would not receive the blessing. If so, why did the secondborn receive the blessing? Because the secondborn was destined to receive the blessing. However, that is not the case. Humanity has been born incorrectly. Therefore, everything that has been born incorrectly must be overturned. Since the starting point was wrong, the wrong starting point must be overturned. We must make a true start from this flawed earth.

Is that starting point meant to repeat the wrong path? No. That would only lead to more wrong results. True results cannot be brought about that way. Therefore, the starting point must be different. That is unavoidable.

For this reason, circumcision was practiced in the Old Testament. When children are circumcised, they are said to be pure and good, right? You may have heard such statements. Why is that? That is the problem. To put it simply, it means that one reaps what one sows. All results must manifest through their causes. So, did humanity's ancestors sow well at the beginning? They sowed incorrectly. What did they sow incorrectly? It was not the tree of the knowledge of good and evil that was sown incorrectly. It was not the seed of a tree that bears good fruit that was sown incorrectly. It was the flawed love that was sown incorrectly. Because flawed love was sown incorrectly, in the end, the fruits of flawed love will inevitably be harvested globally.

When did Adam and Eve fall? They fell during their adolescent years. They sowed flawed love during their adolescent years. They did not sow principled love. It is through that flawed love that humanity was born. Therefore, the time must come when it must be harvested.

Today, wherever you go in the world, the biggest social issue is the ethical problems of youth. Why do these young people act out in ways that lead to their own downfall? It is because the seeds that Adam and Eve sowed have borne fruit, and now it is time to harvest. What Adam and Eve sowed must yield results according to the law of cause and effect, and it must be resolved. This is why such phenomena are occurring globally, as the laws of the universe dictate.

Thus, flawed love has been sown. Because they were born through flawed love, they were all born as false sons. Therefore, God must send true sons to save humanity, which has become false sons. As soon as God sends a true son, it is absolutely not the case that He can save the entire world at once. It must be done through lineage. Because humanity has been born from the lineage of Satan, it must be cut off, trampled, and disregarded in order to be reborn anew. For this reason, God has been working throughout history to change that lineage.

In the presence of the subject of love, it is a principle to be in a position of being governed.
When viewed from the perspective of one person, Adam, God, as the Creator who created Adam, is in a position to claim him according to principle. How did Satan come to be in a position to claim Adam? Did he drag him away by eating the fruit of the tree of the knowledge of good and evil? No, he could not. Because he established a relationship with Adam based on love, Adam could not help but be drawn in.

Originally, when viewed through the lens of the principle of creation, once a love connection is established, one must inevitably be governed by the other. One enters into the realm of that person's dominion. This is true when a love relationship is formed. For example, if a young man in a certain neighborhood establishes a loving relationship with the eldest daughter of a wealthy family, even if that young man is a scruffy servant from another household, that wealthy daughter will inevitably be caught up with him. No matter how much she tries to escape, she cannot. Once that young man declares his love, no matter how wealthy the daughter is, she will inevitably be governed by him. The law of love dictates that being governed is the principle.

However, it was Satan who first established a relationship with humanity based on love. By Adam and Eve entering into the dominion of Satan, Satan could boldly claim Adam and Eve as his own. Therefore, from the standpoint of God, who is in a principled position, He must completely make Adam and Eve His own, but since Satan has established a relationship based on love, he has the content to completely govern Adam and Eve, leading to a conflict between God and Satan. Both sides are claiming that Adam and Eve belong to them.

It is a principle that once a love connection is established, one must be governed, and God, who established this principle, cannot deny it. If God were to eliminate Satan because he intervened unlawfully, it would mean abolishing the very principle of love that God Himself established. Therefore, that cannot happen. All historical issues arise from this point. Thus, the providential history of salvation is to separate Adam and Eve and repair what is broken as if it were not broken.

The principle is that the one who loves first governs the other. This is the law of love. So, who loved first? It was the archangel and Eve. Then, Eve and Adam established their relationship. When viewed through the principle of creation, God is in a position to govern Adam and Eve, but based on love, Satan must govern them.

The purpose of the separation providence from the family of Adam
So, what must be done? Since the law of love has been reversed, it must be restored according to the principle. To do this, Adam must be divided into God's side and Satan's side, but since directly cutting Adam would lead to his death, it must be done through Adam's sons. Adam's sons are the fruits of love, so they can be governed by both God and Satan. Therefore, Cain and Abel must be separated into God's side and Satan's side. The first love is the love between the archangel and Eve, so the firstborn Cain is placed on Satan's side as a representation of that love, and the second love is the love between Eve and Adam, so the secondborn Abel is placed on God's side as a representation of that love.

The outcome of this battle is not determined by God or Satan. The fall was caused by Satan, but the one who fell is humanity, so the victory or defeat of the battle lies with humanity itself. Whether the providence of salvation is achieved or not is determined by human actions. Therefore, God began the providence of salvation from the family of Adam.

Originally, Adam is the son of God, and the archangel is the servant of God. The servant must completely obey and submit to the son of God. However, the servant, the archangel, has become the one who governs Adam, who is the son. The archangel governed Adam and Eve. In other words, the principle of dominion has been reversed. Therefore, this must be restored.

Originally, Adam, who stood on God's side, was supposed to govern Eve and the archangel based on God's love and establish the principles of heaven. However, due to Adam's fall, while God is in a position to claim Adam based on the principle of creation, based on love, Satan has come to be in a position to claim Adam.

To restore this to God's side, what must be done? Since the archangel, who should be governed, has reversed the situation and governed Adam, it is necessary to return to the original standard by entering into a position of being governed. Thus, Cain, who was placed on Satan's side, must submit to Abel, who was placed on God's side. If he does not submit, restoration cannot occur. This is the first trace of God's providential history.

Yet, Abel is misunderstood for offering a blood sacrifice, and people say various things about it, but that is not the point. Why is a blood sacrifice necessary? It is necessary because of the fall. Because of the fall, a blood sacrifice is needed. 

So, how do we return to the state before the fall? Fundamentally, the positions must be reversed. Thus, Cain must go before God through Abel, and also...
The leader must go before God through Adam. The standard of being a fallen archangel, in other words, the archangel who was supposed to receive dominion centered on God's love from Adam and Eve, ended up reversing the dominion by dominating Adam and Eve. This must be properly established. Therefore, the firstborn was set on the side of Satan, and the later-born was set on the side of heaven, in order to correct the wrongs that had occurred by swapping the positions of the later-born and the firstborn.

When we look at the fallen people of this world and Jesus, all fallen people are ultimately in the position of the fallen Adam, which is the position of Cain. However, Jesus is in the position of Abel, the second Adam, who was born as the later-born. Thus, through Jesus, the positions of Cain and Abel are swapped.

Because Satan first exercised the authority of dominion centered on love from the position of the firstborn, the younger brother can automatically be dominated as well. Therefore, God has carried out the work of taking back what was lost. Jacob stole the birthright from Esau with a bowl of stew, but how could such a cunning trickster like Jacob become the one to receive the holy blessing of the three generations: the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob? The reason is that Jacob was a trickster, but that was necessary for the restoration through indemnity. Since the elder brother caused the problem, the younger brother must restore it.

Without the authority to subjugate Satan, one cannot enter heaven. Is it true that all 66 books of the Bible are intertwined with this content, and that by blindly believing without understanding, one can go to heaven? Absolutely not. If one could go to heaven by believing blindly, the teacher would not have been enduring opposition and persecution all this time. The teacher is not doing this because of incompetence. I have pushed through, understood, and investigated. The content they know is fundamentally different from the origin of thought. Unless this is clarified and the root corrected, the purpose of the providence of salvation for humanity cannot be achieved. In other words, humanity cannot receive salvation. Therefore, the firstborn must be rejected, and the later-born must take away the authority of the firstborn.

Thus, in the family of Adam, it was intended to establish this centered on Cain and Abel, but Cain killed Abel, resulting in Satan invading Adam again, which repeated the content of the fall. Therefore, the will was not fulfilled and has been prolonged. Why has the absolute God not been able to fulfill the providence of salvation for 6,000 years, leading people to say that God is powerless or that God is dead? Why has He been put in a position where He cannot move? What kind of God is that? Even a president of a country, once a law is enacted and announced to the people, cannot escape the law himself.

The problem arose because Cain, on the side of Satan, killed Abel, who was on the side of heaven. Originally, Abel was supposed to subjugate Cain and place Satan in submission before humanity, but instead, Cain, on the side of Satan, killed Abel, who was on God's side, repeating the position that led to the fall of the archangel Adam. Thus, the will has been prolonged without finding a resolution in history. God has been carrying out the providence of restoration until now.

God attempted to carry out the providence of restoration centered on the two sons of Adam but failed. This was repeated with Isaac, centered on Esau and Jacob. Jacob initially stole the birthright from Esau with a promise of stew, and then he took it away in reality. The 21 years of living in Haran were a period of struggle to reclaim that birthright.

Thus, the younger brother Jacob, returning to his hometown, should be welcomed by the elder brother Esau. However, Jacob could not simply be welcomed. Therefore, at the Jabbok River, he wrestled with an angel and had to indemnify the fact that the ancestor of humanity, Adam, was subjugated by the archangel. A person cannot enter heaven without subjugating an angel. By wrestling with the angel through the night at the Jabbok River, Jacob established the standard that opened the way for humanity to return to God's side. Without the authority to subjugate Satan, one cannot return as God's sons and daughters. Moreover, without subjugating not only Satan but also the numerous angels in the spiritual realm, one cannot return as God's sons and daughters.

So why is Satan feared? Originally, Satan is an archangel, and we humans are God's children, so angels are our servants. But why should a servant be feared? It is because they have deviated from principle. No matter how wealthy a person may be, if they commit a sin and are cast out, they fall into a position worse than that of a servant. Therefore, humanity must indemnify the fact that they were subjugated by Satan and, at some point, subjugate Satan again. If such content is not found in the Bible, then the Bible cannot be a scripture that saves humanity.

The reason Esau and Jacob were born as twins. However, Jacob, while spending the night at the Jabbok River, fought and won against the angel, establishing such a condition. But why did the angel strike Jacob's hip? Why did he strike the hip bone among many bones? It is because the hip bone was misused, leading humanity to fall. In other words, it is because love was misused that the fall occurred. The Bible records that when the Israelites made an oath, they placed their hands on their hip bones, and this was all for that reason. Humanity's ancestor fell by misusing love, and he vowed never to stand in that position again. This symbolizes that Adam fell due to wrongful love. It is the same before God.

Today, there are terms like "red" and "leftist," where "leftist" refers to the side of Satan. The term "red" indicates danger. This must be confessed before God. There is no limit to discussing such content. Cain and Abel were born separately and fought, but in the time of Jacob, they were born as twins and fought. The form of the struggle changed slightly. In the time of Cain and Abel, the restoration was attempted centered on brothers born separately, but in the time of Esau and Jacob, it was attempted centered on brothers born as twins. So does victory there mean that God's will is fully accomplished? Not at all. Originally, humans are not born as twins; it is normal to be born alone. So why were they born as twins? It is because the son on the side of Satan knocked down the son on God's side, ultimately to take away the position of the firstborn.

In the family of Adam, Cain and Abel were born separately as brothers, indicating a greater distance between them. However, twins are born only a few minutes apart. God shortened the distance between the elder and younger brothers. Humans are born from their mother's womb. So why does God work through twins? Because Cain is also a son of Adam, and Abel is also a son of Adam, they were divided into the sides of heaven and Satan, so God made them fight again in the same womb. There, the younger brother must win and come out in the position of the firstborn to establish the standard to dominate everything. To win in the fight, one must ultimately return to the womb. One must go down step by step and find the basis of victory in the womb; otherwise, the standard of restoration of the firstborn cannot be established.

Thus, the history of the Bible is a history that pushes into the womb. Therefore, Esau and Jacob were different from the time of Cain and Abel. Thus, Esau and Jacob fought from the womb. If the younger brother, who is on God's side, subjugates the elder brother, who is on Satan's side, restoration happens automatically.

Today, when we say to believe in Jesus absolutely, it means to absolutely subjugate Satan. You may have been born after Jesus, but bloodline-wise, you were born with the blood of Adam, who fell and became aligned with Satan, so you belong to the fallen Adam. To put it in terms of trees, Adam is a several-thousand-year-old tree, and you are the leaves of that old tree. No matter how capable someone may seem, they are still part of that lineage. It cannot be helped, even if it is disappointing.

Jesus came 2,000 years ago, but in terms of the fundamental position in which He was born, He is in the position of the younger brother, born after us. Therefore, we must submit to Jesus, who is our younger brother, and honor Him as our elder brother and the King of Kings. Jesus was the King among many kings in the fallen world, but He is the King of Kings and the Father of all humanity. In other words, He is in the position of a parent.

A new history unfolded through Jacob's victory. If Jacob had lost while wrestling with the angel at the Jabbok River, what would have happened? He would have been killed by his brother. However, because he spiritually subjugated the angel there, many ancestors in the spiritual world also stood on Jacob's side. Thus, because Esau welcomed Jacob, who stood on the foundation of spiritual victory, a standard was established to carry out God's will. By welcoming Jacob, Esau enabled Jacob to restore the birthright.

In the past, Cain killed Abel, but Esau did not kill Jacob, who was in a position like that of an enemy; instead, he welcomed him, allowing history to turn back from there. The history that had been prolonged as the source of death due to the fighting between brothers was adorned with a new page through the reconciliation of Jacob and Esau, from which the name Israel emerged.

Jacob and Esau fought after being born and raised, and Jacob won. However, originally, they should have fought and won from the womb before being born.
