There are those who retreat, those who fall back and then rise again to continue their journey, and those who repeatedly stumble while walking their path.

The Importance of Earthly Life
So, how is your walk? What kind of line are you drawing in your life? Are you living a life that God can see, protect, and be with you in, and are you walking the path that God has presented? This is a very serious matter. If you live a life that God wants to hold onto and sympathize with, and if you live in a place where God cannot help but remember you when you face difficulties on your path, then you will remain on this earth as a necessary person before God and will receive eternal care.

But in what manner are you walking this path? Is what you are doing a minus before God or a plus? Are you in debt to the church or are you causing the church to be in debt? This question will determine whether you stand in a place of glory before God or in a place of unhappiness. You must understand that this is being repeated every hour you spend. Thus, you should live today in such a way, and plan to live tomorrow in such a way, and since you lived this year in such a manner, you must plan to live next year in such a manner, ensuring that you leave something behind. You must leave something behind.

Time does not stand still. It does not flow as you wish. Time flows along with your age. The age of purpose also flows. Your age flows as well. So how will you shape the flowing fortune of heaven, the flowing time, and the flowing life of ours? How will you align the path that God walks with the path that I walk, and how will you connect that with the fortune of the world? If you cannot connect them, you must prepare a time to connect them, even if it means holding back the flow. When you think of this, it is not a simple problem. You must understand that you cannot do this with an ordinary daily life.

Since you have been born, you must go, and you must leave something behind as you go. You must not go in debt but rather leave a legacy. You must leave a legacy before that nation. It may sound strange to say that you are leaving a legacy, but in any case, you must give something to this world as you leave. If there are people who have been like this in the past, are like this now, and will be like this in the future, then the history of the past will be settled because of them, the present will be settled because of them, and the future will also be settled because of them.

God is eternal. He is eternal in the past, present, and future. However, even if God is eternal, if He causes loss in the world and before heaven and earth, then that God cannot become the eternal being that humanity desires. The eternal God, through the past, present, and future, is always in a position to provide necessary, appropriate, and valuable content to humanity, or the created world, or the world of existence. Therefore, you must understand that God was needed in the past, is needed in the present, and will be needed in the future. If such content does not exist for us, then that eternal God has no relation to us. Moreover, the very desire to revere that God, to belong to that God, and to establish a relationship with that God cannot be without contradiction.

Therefore, in seeking eternal life and in our desire to possess eternal life, we must be as God was in the past, as God is in the present, and as God will be in the future. You must understand that you must leave something behind according to your circumstances, knowing that you can coexist with the eternal God of the past, present, and future.

When a parent works hard for their child, that effort remains in the child's heart, and the child is grateful to the parent until death. Likewise, if someone sacrifices their life for the country and leaves something behind, people will remember them forever. And if there is a sage who has devoted their heart to the world and left something behind, the people of the world will remember them.

So what will we leave behind in the eternal life journey of God? What will we leave in the eternal living environment that God longs for and hopes for? It is a matter of leaving something, whether external or internal. Looking at my own characteristics, I find that I have nothing prepared. However, I must leave this one thing behind. There must be something I can do. This is necessary in the past, present, and future. Therefore, it must also be necessary for the eternal God. Thus, we will eternally accompany the eternal God who possesses such attributes.

You must each strive to leave something that you can do. Leaving something means creating your own wealth. The path you are walking is a path of competition. Therefore, you must adorn that path as you go. You will eventually come before God. However, the path to reach the Father is the final path of destiny that you must walk alone. If you walk that path and God does not welcome you, have you ever thought about what you would do? When you are born into this world, do you want to be born as a lonely reader or as a child of someone who has nothing, in such a pitiful situation? You probably do not want that. Everyone wishes to be born into a wealthy environment, that is, a wealthy family or a wealthy nation. They wish to be born in such a fortunate environment that can welcome and embrace them from the moment they are born.

When we see this, we must understand what kind of appearance we will have and in what kind of country we will be born. Will we be born in a wealthy environment, or will we be born in a way that the entire universe, heaven and earth, can welcome? We must understand that this short life journey determines our fate.

In the future, we will face the second world. That world is a world we must go to. We must be reborn and enter that world. The question remains whether we will enter as a lonely reader or into a wealthy environment that can welcome our birth.

So what does the church teach? It teaches that by living in this way on earth, we can have a wealthy environment in the other world. You must understand that this applies to both internal and external lives. So did you have such motivation by entering the church? To enter the church means to be connected here. You were born here, grew up here, and will live here until one day you leave. You must keep in mind what you will leave behind, knowing that you were born on the foundation of God's hard work over the past 2,000 years and that you have relied on the church until now.

Leaving something behind does not mean giving it to someone else. It becomes your foundation. It is your foundation. Just as a person born into a good family inherits everything from their parents, that becomes your wealth. It is something that no one can take away from you.

Similarly, when you go to that world, will you be able to maintain such an environment? At what point in this life journey will you establish a connection with God? Also, at what point will everyone take an interest in you, praise what you enjoy, and share in what you like? You must always think and feel about these things as you go through your life journey.

Among people, there are two types: those who are born into happy circumstances and live happily, and those who are born into sad circumstances and live sadly. However, this can interchange; even those born into joyful environments will go through sadness, and those born into sad circumstances will also experience joy. You must consider how you will ultimately go and at what times you will seek such things in your life. You must recognize that your actions are to prepare for such moments and that you must take a special interest in them.

<Prayer> Today is May 11, 1969, the second Sunday of this month. Since the day I unfolded my existence in the world of being, battles have arisen while connecting space and time, and I am still engaged in fierce battles.

At this time, we have gathered before you to think about what we should do. I have come here. I have fought like this and will continue to do so. The past was like this, today is like this, and tomorrow will be like this. I long for the time when I can connect with you and follow you into the battlefield where you fight, and I must go through this fierce world of struggle.

We are humble and weak beings. Standing alone in the desolate wilderness, fearing the attack of wild beasts, may we be your children who can think of the place where Jacob gathered his lonely heart while heading toward Haran.

Even if no one is around, if it becomes a place where God can intervene and where you can dwell, then there is a motive for life and eternal joy, and we must surely know this.

Father, in what manner will we joyfully call upon you? Is there a time when we have called upon you with blood in our veins and the heartbeat of our heart's arteries at their peak? Let us reflect on what kind of place we have called upon you. We must be your children who will work for you in any place and who will dedicate this body and this life completely.

We know that those who live without leaving a trace and meaningfully departing are not needed before heaven. Such people are also not needed in the human world. They are not needed in families either. It is only natural that what is needed is not the ordinary appearance of living like that, but people who lead families, nations, and the world while struggling. Therefore, we must become your sons and daughters who strive for the church and for your will today and tomorrow. Thus, if we repeat that path for ten days, a year, or a lifetime, we will meet a day of glory that is praised in place of heaven, and if we walk for humanity, we will be honored in place of humanity.

Let us realize once again the important question of how many days we will leave behind for humanity on this earth, how many years we will leave as days that humanity can remember, and what kind of death we will face, a question that we must never forget as we live our lives.

We have seen that while some people struggle for heaven, feeling the painful heart of the Father alone, there are also those who ridicule them. Father! We have seen many people who came to you with joyful faces, raising their hands and shouting praises, only to disappear without a trace. We have clearly seen how joyful faces turn into faces of enemies and hatred, cursing you. Each time we feel this, the painful heart that is remembered is lonelier and more miserable than anyone else's heart in the world. Whenever we feel such things, we think of how you have endured even greater hardships.

We, who must pioneer the path of destiny that we must walk, resolve to make these enemies repent before you. If we do not take ourselves as a source of re-starting from this place, we must become children who clearly understand that we cannot escape from the same fate.

As I think about what I have left behind, I block the sorrow of heaven and say, "Heaven! Please believe in me." At the same time, let us know how much you are longing for and searching for someone who can take responsibility for the path you walk and lead the whole way.

We know that those who watch, ridicule, and criticize those who are going toward you will naturally drift away and fall away from you. The farther we go, the more we must make new resolutions and leave behind achievements in the path of struggle. Let us be assured that the achievements left by those who have struggled for you will give rise to the founding of a holy new world.

Please take care of this entire day from this morning. To the lonely sons and daughters scattered across the world! Please bless the sincere appearances of those who long for their teacher a thousand times over. Bestow the gift of glory upon the children who are fighting to find you so that they do not become dropouts in the current struggle.
I earnestly ask you to hold on. May we be children who can fulfill the responsibilities entrusted to us before heaven. I have prayed all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *

18)
Let us not be burden-bearers
It is a good thing for you to convey news to those who are abroad or to contact them. 
Letters are good, but they must be written well. 
When a country is in crisis, if the entire content of that crisis is communicated to the citizens, it can cause problems with their morale. If a country is in crisis and people think that this crisis will end the nation, it cannot recover from that crisis. If a country is in crisis, there must be someone who can take responsibility for that crisis. The person who takes responsibility to overcome that crisis must be more thoughtful than anyone else. Those who merely observe and comment do not understand the position of the person who has taken responsibility. Therefore, when you are faced with a crisis, you should not just say "crisis, crisis," but even if you are in a crisis, you must instill new hope that can overcome that environment. Only when such new movements are connected can the crisis be overcome. 
However, among those who write letters, there are many who deserve divine punishment. The church is not something that is solely the responsibility of an individual. Yet, to speak as if one is responsible for the church is an extremely fearful thing. 
May 11, 1969 (Sunday), former headquarters church.
* This message was given after the dawn worship, but the earlier part was not recorded. The title was added by the editor.

There are countless times when the teacher faces environmental challenges in his work. He is attacked from all sides and is buffeted by winds from all directions. In such an environment, if one only hopes for the slightest news from the headquarters, that the headquarters is doing well and developing, to evaluate how the headquarters is doing is like cutting one's own throat. If it is due to the teacher's special mission, it may be understandable, but writing unnecessary letters and saying things that are not true is not acceptable. Those who do such things are all wanderers who have not settled down. If this kind of gossip continues, God cannot do anything about the immature headquarters team. 
When the teacher goes on a tour, the most troublesome thing is that. Unexpected words, things the teacher never thought of, and statements that do not match the facts are all written in letters. Who asked for such letters to be written? There are countless people who act as if they are responsible and are being pointed at by others. 
Moreover, there are those who are discussing this and that with close people. Such people must be completely cleared away at some point in the future. To the extent that the teacher knows, everything must be cleared away and moved on. In the future, such historical events will become significant issues in the touring process. Moreover, did the teacher create the motives for events that could become problematic in the second seven-year course? Or did someone else create them? This too must be cleared away in the unfolding of history. People who are not responsible in the church act as if they are responsible. This is an extreme contradiction. 
In the pioneering era, there are difficulties from the very beginning. The struggle in pioneering is difficult from the start. However, the person in charge must overcome those difficulties. They must carry on with the conviction to overcome those difficulties. Yet, there are those who do not participate and write letters from a third-party perspective. Why do they write letters that inflict fatal wounds on those who are working hard? Instead of giving hope and encouragement, why do they cause pain? I think we need to control sending letters abroad from now on. 
Let us not be burden-bearers
A letter should be something that encourages the recipient and adds value to their path. A letter that does not do this is worthless. Why cause conflict in the heart of someone who is trying to be loyal to the cause without knowing anything? There are many such people. The responsibility is not yours to bear. However, you must be equipped with the ability to take responsibility. 
The teacher does not write letters. He does not write them often because he worries it may become a burden. It is not the leaders who do it either; it is the wanderers of the Unification Church who write letters that create such terrible misunderstandings, and this cannot be forgiven. 
Even when writing letters, good content must be included. The headquarters must convey good news as much as possible. For those who follow, this is not possible. When something good happens in America, the people in charge did not reach that position comfortably. They endured far more hardships internally to get to that point. They must endure even more hardships. Those who follow can turn back or take a detour if things go badly. However, those who lead cannot take a detour just because things are bad. Even if it is bad, they must digest it and move on. They must go through intense internal suffering. That is why those who take responsibility face many difficulties. 
Do not be a burden to the church
Whether in Japan, Europe, or America, members in intermediate positions go back and forth among themselves discussing this and that. This is the same in America or anywhere else. Because we are in the world of faith, we must always speak words that can support each other in our faith lives. Instead of saying such words, they listen to useless stories from somewhere and discuss this and that. Generally, many of those people have fallen away. They have all fallen away from the church. Such people are bound to fall away. 
What are the problems of the church? Although everything belonging to the church should be respected, they claim, "This is my father's, so it is mine." There are all sorts of characters. 
If you want to develop in the future, do not ask for recognition of your hard work. "I have worked for the church, so the church should help me." Such a person is a merchant. They are someone who is doing business with God on this earth. A person who thinks, "I have worked hard for the church, so the church should help me," will not be helped even if they ask for help. They forget that they have become a traitor, forget the intense pioneering path the church has taken, and try to leave their burdens behind. They do not consider that they are obstructing the path of the church. In this regard, wisdom is necessary. You must think. 
The Unification Church members must not become a burden anymore. Although I welcomed you today, if you meet the teacher, do not become a burden to him. Do not impose your burdens on the church. You must never impose your own burdens on the church. You should bear the burdens of the church from a public standpoint but not impose personal burdens on it. However, there are many complaints even when they should be bearing burdens from a public standpoint. 
When you look at foreigners, it is not like that. What is the difference between Westerners and Easterners? Westerners have a strong spirit of independence. By the age of 18, they are already expected to be self-reliant. This is established as a thorough educational policy. However, the East is not like that. This is the turning point that creates the current worldview. The spirit of independence means that one will pioneer and find their own way. 
Of course, one may receive help from the church from a public standpoint, but there are standards that God looks at. Because of the times we are in, there are clear standards for what efforts must be made, and if one forgets those standards and becomes a position that can cause concern before those standards, it is not good. Therefore, you must learn to regard such aspects as enemies. 
Let us not be burden-bearers
In a public path, if an individual seeks personal gain, all corruption arises from there. Misfortunes occur. In public matters, one should contribute; otherwise, it is not public. If one seeks personal gain in public matters, they will fail. Organizations with many such people will perish. Countries with many such citizens will also perish. Is it acceptable for everyone to just seek their own benefit without regard for the nation or anything else? If one becomes indebted to public matters, that country or individual will quickly perish. One must be in a position where they are not ashamed before heaven and earth in everything from one to ten. If one becomes indebted in such a position, heaven will repay them all. Those who live this way will never find themselves in a position of indebtedness. Rather, they will be in a position to give. 
On the path of the will, one must always bear the cross
Although you lead your family, you must always be in a public position. In your heart, life, and actions, you must strive to work from a public standpoint more than anyone else. Who would like someone who is neither this nor that? Long-time members may be indifferent, but I intend to separate long-time members into about twenty different groups. I will continue to separate them. Only by separating can both survive. It is like grafting. Even with trees, species like the willow need to be pruned. If left alone, they will wither. However, if you mercilessly prune them from the beginning, both the tree and the branches will thrive and become new trees. If left alone, the tree will die due to the rotten branches. 
That is why you must always carry a cross on the path of the will. You must carry the lonely cross. Because of that, you may be more troubled and unable to relax than ever, but you will be dignified. Such a person will never fail in anything they do. Their time will surely come. When I see long-time members giving testimonies, it is good when the testimony is given by someone who is fighting with a conviction greater than when they were active. However, giving a testimony with a heart that has already faded away can lead to anger. Why does it lead to anger? Because hearing that testimony does not inspire the masses to do the same; instead, it tries to mold the masses in their own way to gain sympathy, which can lead to great anger. 
"I did this, so you all must go this way. I suffered like this, so you must repay me." This cannot be the case. 
To testify about the past, one must also be prepared to testify about today. In this way, the past and today must create a reciprocal standard. A testimony that does not do this is worse than not giving one at all. It becomes empty. In other words, no matter how well one did in the past, a single mistake can make them a traitor. No matter how many times one did well in the past, breaking the law even once will catch up with them. That is why this public position is extremely lonely and, if it is frightening, it is a very frightening position. One can never relax, eat, or live comfortably in such a position. You must understand that. That is the secret of life. Evangelism is the same. 
What can create the world of principles?
Because humans are spiritual beings, when there is someone who leads them stronger than anyone else and embraces them emotionally, they want to be drawn into that embrace. Your prayers are also about extending such times. It is nothing else. You pray to extend such times. 
If you have a longing to see someone more and pray for them while they are sleeping, and wish for blessings for them, it extends the time you can be together. When you meet someone who has prayed for you like that, you cannot express how happy you are. Imagine waiting for them to come without sleeping at night. Then they will come without sleeping. They will be drawn in. The teacher is the same. Wherever he goes, when he reaches that level, even if night falls, drowsiness is not an issue. When the stimulation from another world, that is, the emotional stimulation stronger than drowsiness, interacts with him, drowsiness becomes irrelevant. When the stimulation is stronger than fatigue, that fatigue becomes nothing. You may know the principles of strength, but without that heart, evangelism will never happen. 
Therefore, when a person arrives, you should not think, "Why did that person come? I don't want to see them." You must not think that way. Even when meeting an enemy, you should not think of them as an enemy. You must be able to interact without distance. But how many people can do that? Think about it. You must be able to conquer even the world of enemies. A person who has the motivation to conquer enemies without fighting and silently win them over to their side is called a sage. 
You should not be complacent or hang around with those who do not understand the will, even if you know it. You should not live with someone you do not welcome. If you do, you will begin to separate from that connection. When such hearts gather, they will cause accidents. They will cause accidents. Evangelism is the same. When you meet, you should be happy and talk all night, and when you are apart, you should miss each other. If those who live together cannot miss each other, they are not worth living together. 
Now is a different time. There are no enemies before you, so it is a different time. Therefore, you set the condition that you have won and go out when the time comes. In the future, those who cannot take responsibility will not be used at the headquarters. Those close to the teacher must be people who have fulfilled their responsibilities according to the principles. Those who have not fulfilled their responsibilities according to the principles will absolutely not be given positions as department heads, district leaders, or regional leaders. Therefore, unless one has gone through the official path according to the principles, they cannot be close to the headquarters or the teacher. This applies to the 36 families and all other families in the future. Those who have not acted according to the principles cannot be close to the teacher. You must understand this clearly. 
In the future, if you want to create the world of principles, what will you use to create that world if it is not based on principles? The same goes for the headquarters. Only those who have fulfilled their responsibilities can enter. Just as one must establish a family to enter heaven, one must fulfill their responsibilities to enter the headquarters. In the future, the teacher will decide on greetings to the headquarters based on the condition that responsibilities have been fulfilled. Those who cannot fulfill their responsibilities, even if they are department heads or something else, must not complain about their hardships in the future. From now on, even department heads who cannot take responsibility will be sent away. They will all be sent away to fulfill their responsibilities. If they cannot pave their own way, the teacher will be held accountable in the next world. 
That is why those who cannot take responsibility must pack their bags and leave. Even district leaders will be transferred to local areas to pioneer and evangelize to pave their own way. They must fulfill their responsibilities. The same goes for the headquarters. 
You may wonder what responsibilities there are at the headquarters, but that is absolutely not the case. Is it acceptable to have three children of principled faith and not have evangelized twelve people while being at the headquarters? That does not make sense. Evangelism can be done through letters or advice. A letter can be read, right? 
Can a woman be born and not get married? Can a man be born and not marry?
Is it possible? I cannot not go. A person without a family cannot be a member of society or a citizen of that country. I do not believe in the nation either. What does the principle of the Unification Church teach? It teaches about family. Restoration is not individual restoration but family restoration. It is about restoring the expectation of the son-in-law. The conditions inside and outside that can accomplish this are the nation. However, until now, there has not been a solid ideology established regarding this. (Some parts omitted due to poor recording quality) 

When it comes to the issue of life and death, can you sleep comfortably? If you provoke a reaction when you are tired, that fatigue will be relieved. If you suddenly press down hard, your mind will come back. When you are tired, if you firmly resolve to become even more tired suddenly, there will be a backlash from that. These days, when I quietly observe young people, it is truly strange. They need to sleep for several hours. When the issue of life and death is at stake, they say they will do it after sleeping for a few hours. When dying, do you think it would work to say, "Oh, I will sleep for a few hours before I die"?

When the teacher fled from the North, he had to cross the border near the 38th parallel, and he sensed that the situation was very urgent at that time. Knowing that the border area was dangerous, he tried to cross the border, but the guards did not chase him. If they chased him, they would be pushed back, and if the guards moved forward, they would follow them out. They already knew that it would be disadvantageous for them. So, he saw all the guards retreating on the spot. That night, although he was sleepy, he could not sleep, and his intuition was strange. Sure enough, the guards packed their belongings and fled. At that time, there was no other way but to follow those people. Since they were frontline guards, the teacher knew that they would take the fastest route to escape. He had to follow them. So, he quietly followed them, and they took a boat to Yongmaedo. The distance from Haeju to Cheongdan was about 80 ri, and it was 2 AM at that time. In the urgent situation of whether he could go if he did not retreat with the guards, the teacher was worried to the point of suffocation, but this guy was dozing off while walking. Many people went like that. At that time, the teacher experienced for the first time that one could doze off while walking. (Recording was interrupted) 

Responsibilities of the members in Korea
The members at the headquarters often feel that they wish others would not act that way. You must understand how precious the headquarters is. Members abroad wish they could come to the headquarters and at least serve as watchmen or clean the restrooms. They think they would be grateful to do such work for their whole lives. When they come and pick up a rag and a broom, those living at the headquarters must have a foundation that can inherit that tradition. This is the problem. 

Establishment of an urgent headquarters system
In light of this, you must understand how urgent it is for us to establish a new system for the headquarters. Moreover, this year, not only Japanese people are coming, but several other foreigners are also coming. We plan to bring about ten of them to prepare for new global work. Once these people come, they will already want to enter the headquarters. Seeing this, we can feel anew that the responsibility of the headquarters is heavy. 

On this side of Cheongpah-dong, there is Hyochang Park, and on the other side, there is Seoul Station along the train tracks, and we need to create a detailed map that indicates what is where and send it out to the world. There are many things we have not done until now. Therefore, we must fulfill that responsibility and gradually solve these overall issues. When they arrive at Gimpo Airport, we need to ensure that they can know how to get here and how to walk here in advance, so we must first create a map of the location. Then we can guide them to come. 

When you visit the holy sites in Israel, there is a place where Joseph of Arimathea wrapped the deceased Jesus in linen and sprinkled spices on his face, placing him in a tomb carved into the rock. Some people, having lived in faith for decades, think about the Lord they have longed for in their hearts lying in that tomb and shed tears. However, the people there are only trying to take advantage of those who come there, which is unacceptable. 

After Jesus died, thousands of years have passed, and he has become a historical figure. However, the teacher is currently alive, so when people from around the world gather their intentions to come here to the headquarters, those living at the headquarters must not be indifferent to the teacher. In the usual environment, you cannot be of any help to the teacher. Therefore, I have come to think that in the future, only blessed families should be allowed to enter the headquarters. At least for a few years, they should go out to the local areas, do evangelism, build results, and experience God's heart to some extent. In the future, we should establish the spiritual leaders and allow them to enter after passing through them. Many people are currently preparing for that mission. 

Blessed families must set an example for foreign members
The headquarters church is nothing right now. There are all sorts of people attached to it. That is why we plan to organize it in the future. Furthermore, I am thinking that the teacher will try to hold fewer official gatherings as much as possible in the future. 

Now, the teacher feels that he must teach the norms regarding family life, which should be held as a heavenly family. However, those who must walk the path of restoration should receive teachings through those who can teach based on the principle. The era in which the teacher directly takes responsibility for such issues has passed. We must reorganize around each family. Our Unification Church organization is a family organization. It is centered on families. It means that we are shifting from focusing on individuals to focusing on families. Until now, you have looked down on families. The family you thought was insignificant turns out to be the family you need. 

Just as the stone that was rejected has become the cornerstone, the family you have felt was worthless has now come to the time to appear with absolute authority. This is why blessings are precious. Only those who have been trained like this can confidently face foreign members and teach them through the duties of family and show them an example. They do not know about blessed families because they are not blessed families. 

If you look at each individual, you will lose to them. However, when you move centered on the family, they must bow their heads and learn from you. In light of this, the only thing you can show them right now is the life of this blessed family. You must show that. Therefore, we must prepare this path in the future. 

There are many young people here, but no one comes to clean the floor. Even if the glass is broken, if the teacher deliberately leaves it alone, no one can be found who would change it even if they had to skip their lunch. When you think about it, these are all sacred objects. The headquarters is not only a national scenic spot but also a scenic spot of our church. However, sometimes when you go up the stairs, you see dust. This is shameful. First of all, you must understand that we need to clean the inside and outside of the church. 

Now that the time has come when we can influence not only domestically but also globally, those at the headquarters must always be prepared. Do you understand? "Yes." Therefore, we must strongly organize this headquarters in the future. 

Blessed families must not forget that they are the representatives of the teacher
What is the first thing foreign members are interested in? It is how those who are close to the teacher live. It is about the environment and lifestyle of the leaders who are close to the teacher. However, there are many people among the leaders who do not meet those conditions. There are several leaders who do not even attend Sunday worship, and that cannot be allowed. Such people are already those who are selling out the headquarters. That is scarier than selling it for money. A leader must understand how heavy the burden of being a leader is. Foreign members are very interested in the close aides of the teacher and the leaders of the headquarters. They compare their work centered around the headquarters. Yet, do the people responsible act as if they are indifferent? 

Next, what are they very interested in? They are very interested in the blessed 36 families. They believe that being blessed means moving from the growth stage to the completion stage. Therefore, they think that blessed people are those who can give birth to good sons and daughters who do not believe in the Lord and go straight to heaven. How happy and grateful that must be! Just imagine that. When they see it that way, even in extremely difficult living conditions, they can understand that the heart of devotion for the purpose must be extreme. However, if they do not live that way, there is something powerful that no one can interfere with. 

Aren't you the same? When centered on Jesus, Peter, James, and John are the three disciples, then the twelve disciples, and then the seventy disciples are of interest. So, in our church, there is interest in the seventy-two families, then the one hundred twenty families, and then the four hundred thirty families. Recently, a Chinese person came and left, and you must have heard that he came to see how blessed families actually live, knowing that the principles of the Unification Church are known worldwide. 

When God chooses one person to send as a representative of a nation, that person is sent with a sorrow greater than that of the nation, as an envoy, as an ambassador, and as a special envoy. However, if that person is treated coldly, it will inflict a fatal wound on the kingdom of God. He is a guest of honor above all guests. He is someone who represents history. Who would have thought of such things? 

Therefore, those who come out with the teacher should not just chatter. The person in charge has responsibilities both inside and outside. However, one should not just gather words that can and cannot be used. Therefore, the person responsible must set an example. When asked what you can be an example of, you must earn points. Now, because of this, people will speculate that it must have been the same one year ago, two years ago, three years ago, four years ago, five years ago. You must understand that the time has come for you to be the subject in your family. 

Foreign members are not only interested in the teacher, but they are also interested in how the leaders of the headquarters, whom they have longed for and hoped for, conduct their public lives. How do they establish their living environment? How are they different from themselves? They are interested in these things. Therefore, you, as the person in charge, must be trustworthy and rise to the standards they desire. They know they cannot directly meet the teacher and say this or that, so they study the leaders at their level, whether they are department heads or section heads. In light of such issues, it is now time to establish the system of the headquarters. In the future, we must pay special attention to that aspect. 

Next, when foreign members come, they will observe the environment. They will see how people live, what time they wake up in the morning, or how they manage their household. They will be interested in these things. 

This time, when the teacher visited the factory in Japan, he was impressed by a young member. This young man, who had been employed for about a year and a half, learned everything he had to do within a month of joining the factory and thoroughly investigated every corner of the factory that even the existing employees with experience did not know, and he came to a conclusion. However, this young man is not an expert. He is only twenty-six years old and graduated from high school three years ago. When considering that he accomplished what others in the factory could not even dream of, it is clear that this young man had a lot of interest. He must have seen every piece of metal and every machine. Behind that heart was a strong desire to cherish the factory and to ensure that everything would go through his hands when he got there. It is because he had such determination that he achieved results equivalent to more than three years in just one month. The teacher needs such people in the future. 

The headquarters church will be the focus of interest for foreign members
Now, when foreign members come, they will analyze everything. They will analyze everything from this blackboard to every piece of glass. They will analyze who works here, what their faces look like, and what kind of personalities they have. You must understand that. In the future, you must not make loud noises when you come to this headquarters church. Some people come here and make a fuss, and some even fight and argue. When the teacher is sleeping in the next room, he can hear even the whispers. Such people are targets for purging in the communist party. When will these people ever become human? We must correct everything through education from now on. 

In the future, no one will be able to enter here carelessly. There will come a time when even if you offer millions of dollars to sleep here for one night, it will not be possible. You must understand that. If you go to the Louvre Museum, which has the Mona Lisa painting, you will find that about fifty people are always gathered in front of that painting. I went there recently, and there were all sorts of people standing in front of that painting, regardless of whether they were good-looking or not. They were all people who did not know a thing about art. 

In the future, this Unification Church headquarters will become a historical place. Those who do not know this will never be able to establish a connection here. There will come a time when even if someone comes here and offers to pay millions of dollars for one night, it will not be possible. If that time does not come, the teacher will make it happen. 

However, there are people like boastful goblins who come here, sit on this floor, and then go to another country to brag about it. "Ah, I sat on that floor... But I dozed off a little?" (Laughter) They spent one evening here, and they think that dozing off is something to brag about? "Oh, it was tough! How can someone preach for three hours? Oh, that person must not be hungry. They said not to eat breakfast on Sunday, but three hours went by..." and they say all sorts of things.
Will this be praised in the spirit world? The 13th, 18th, and 30th granddaughters of someone are dozing off, so will the ancestors say, "Yes! Thank you"? You may not know well because you are at a distance from the spirit world, but your ancestors will boast to each other, saying, "Ah, our granddaughter is coming." This is not a joke. They only come to know the teacher's name and plead for their lives when they reach the spirit world. At that time, the teacher is in the most difficult position. The teacher has done all that needs to be done and prays before heaven, and once a line is drawn, he does not look back.

They also boast among themselves when someone's grandson comes to church, saying, "That guy is doing well." However, if he betrays the will and falls away, they will slander you. You may understand through prayer that the spirit world is making great efforts to bring descendants closer to heaven. Yet here, they curse their ancestors and only seek to live well themselves. Therefore, one must die to understand this. There was a grandmother who recently went to the spirit world and asked to be taught the Principle. Is the teacher's word right or wrong? You should die and see. However, it would be nice if one could die and come back to life, but once you die, that's it. Therefore, people say that even if the Unification Church's Reverend Moon makes threats, they are very impressive threats, ones that no one else can make. But they say, "Try dying." Do you think the teacher is saying these things because he has nothing else to do?

When it is time for a full-scale advance, you must make a total advance centered around the mission to restore this nation. The slogan for this year is also a full-scale advance, right? We are playing around with this now, saying, "Oh! A full-scale advance is something only those with talent can do; can a gang of thugs do that?" The gang can only eat and drink. That cannot be the case. Right now, a total mobilization order has been given to our entire Unification Church. Young ladies must participate, grandmothers must participate, and even mothers with babies must participate. This time, the teacher is showing the example of the restoration path, and it cannot be done without flipping over.

With such a heart, I wanted a woman who could truly make me real, even if I had to go to prison. Sometimes, it would be nice if they could show a little understanding, but they do not show any understanding at all. Even when the teacher is over seventy and his body has weakened, he must lean on a cane. This path must be walked no matter what, so even older people must go without sleeping at night. When I see this, the teacher becomes a subject of study.

Now that we have raised the slogan of a full-scale advance, we must start certain evangelistic activities in Seoul and establish a self that heaven can trust. You must understand that you are in such a position. Everyone who has been in the headquarters for more than three years must be sent out for evangelism. The teacher has also been in Korea for too long, so by next year, he should be in America. When I went to America last time, the American members said they would buy the teacher's house for $50,000. The teacher rejected that, saying, "I am not a poor man." I came back saying that it was not because I didn't have money that I couldn't buy it. How does that feel? "It feels good." What is good about it? You should feel ashamed for even a moment! However, the teacher never thinks like that. The teacher simply loves Korea, where he was born.

Now that it is September, the teacher must go abroad again. This time, I must step forward to connect with U.S. senators centered around Washington, D.C. I will step forward with the pride of the Republic of Korea. If you cannot do it, the teacher will take the lead. Until now, I have entrusted everything to you, but from now on, I will stand at the forefront and push them to save them. If Mr. Moon holds a revival in America, many people will flock to it. You must understand that.

The time when the Unification Church is criticized and insulted in Korea has passed. If such criticism arises now, it will disappear without a trace. Do you understand what I mean? You must understand that while the teacher is here, you must stand in a position to follow the teacher's commands. You cannot imagine how precious it is that when you went to that country, you listened to and followed the teacher's commands a hundred or a thousand times. In the not-so-distant future, there will come a time when commands will not be given, no matter how much you wish for them. You will see whether it is a lie or the truth.

Now is the most precious time. You must meet the second seven-year course. Now that the time has come to be active centered around Seoul, you must welcome it with a united heart of gratitude. Since this is a historical time, I hope you will put forth your utmost sincerity to establish the conditions for victory at this historical moment, just as the teacher has walked. Do you understand?

The head of the general affairs department must create a championship trophy. One for use in Seoul, one for use in the provinces, and one for use worldwide—these three must be created. This is to create the second world tour commemorative trophy. What will we do with this? We will hold competitions for it in the future. Each church will hold a competition once a month with this trophy.

If a church does not attend even once in a year, they will all be punished by bringing a piece of rice cake to worship. They will be allowed to eat well and prepare songs. At that time, the teacher will definitely attend. However, it is not enough for just one person to attend. Each church must have at least 40 people. If there are fewer than 40, they cannot attend. Do you understand? So if there are fewer than 40, you must work hard even if it means staying up all night. Even then, if there are fewer than 40, you cannot come empty-handed. You must bring something, even if it is just snacks. We will continue this for the first, second, and third times, going through all twelve months of the year.

In the future, the teacher will carry out these activities from Seoul to all the churches across the nation and even to every corner of the globe. Even if you only need to evangelize 40 people, you can do it by evangelizing just ten households. However, we must be careful about one thing: as I instructed in the previous operation plan in Japan, do not be greedy. Do not think that you can do everything at once. That will absolutely not work. A day accumulates into a year. You cannot try to do in one day what should be built up over ten years.

From now on, what responsibility does a member of the Unification Church have? To evangelize one person a month. Do not do two people. Just focus on one person a month and put your heart into it. Do not go to other houses; focus on just one house and dedicate yourself daily, sharing the Principle and aiming to restore one person a month. Do you understand? If you do that, how many people will it be in a year? It will be 12, right? You cannot do more than 12, and you cannot do less than 12.

If you only manage to evangelize ten people in a year, you must fast for two months to fill the 12. If you fail to evangelize one person in a month, you must fast for that month, and everyone will do it. This operation has been used in Japan as well. Our methods of operation are now different from the past. When giving birth, if you give birth to twins at once, it is that much harder.

In the future, we will not engage in such games. However, since this is still the restoration era, the Unification Church must be active now. That is why we say to evangelize one person a month. You eat three meals a day, so pray for them before you eat. If possible, shed tears and pray for them for two days during the week. Then, you will surely be able to evangelize. Do you understand? If it still doesn’t work, come and protest to the teacher. Pray with the heart of a parent, shedding tears for that one life. Then, you will surely be able to evangelize. If you evangelize one person a month, and if we are ten thousand people, how many will it be after a year? It will be 120,000. After two years, it will be 1.2 million, and after three years, it will be 12 million. This is how our numbers will grow tenfold each year. If that happens, the restoration of Korea will not be a problem. Keeping this in mind, we must march forward with the goal of evangelizing one person a month.

Let us advance armed with Unification Thought. The teacher said that when the Tokyo University incident occurred in Japan, he gathered the leaders and gave the order to reclaim Tokyo University, which was suffering from leftist student demonstrations. There are about 20 of our students at Tokyo University, and he instructed that each of them should be responsible for ten people. He said not to talk about the Principle study group or the Unification Church's principles there. So what should they do? The students must study. However, if they only engage in demonstrations, a year will pass, and then two years will pass... When they try to graduate and go out, their youthful years will have slipped away. So, if there is someone preventing them from studying, they should be beaten to death.

By doing this, if one person gathers ten comrades, it will become 200. Train these 200 people and put them into 200 classes; if you can attract just the class leaders, creating 1,000 or 2,000 people will not be a problem. Once this is established, the entire student body will say, "Let’s study, and let’s beat to death the communists who prevent us from studying." If we make meticulous plans in this regard and dig in, their organization will collapse. If that happens, the left-leaning Asahi newspaper may attack our ethnic group. However, we have also prepared logical plans for that. If it is not the Unification Church members, there will be no one to save Japan from them.

In the same way, even though the North Korean communists are in a desperate situation due to war, if all the people are armed with the Unification Church's ideology, when they confront them, will they retreat or advance? "We will advance." They must advance. By arming 700,000 people at the front and 2.5 million people in the rear with Unification Thought, it will be as easy as gently guiding fish into a net from a drought-stricken reservoir. The war in Korea will soon become a war in Asia.

Then, we will push all the Chinese communists into the border of the Soviet Union and Manchuria. Wasn't Manchuria once our land? We will reclaim that. Thus, the time will come for us to achieve northern unification.

At some point, the highest leader of this country will come to meet me. The teacher has already set up all the operations for that. So, I am already doing such work from abroad. If I say to mobilize someone in Taiwan or someone in Japan, they will immediately prepare for it and all stand in the position of being responsible. The entire Unification Church in Japan is also doing this now.

Monthly evangelism for everyone. The entire Unification Church in Japan has been instructed to carry out the movement to restore just one person a month, not even two. The restoration of Korea is not a problem. One-third of the 30 million people are children, and another third are the elderly, so the young people, those in their 20s to 40s, number only ten million. However, do not feel sad if you are older. As long as your heart is young, that is enough. Let’s do one person evangelism a month. Do you understand? If you are at work, evangelize at work; if you are in a factory, evangelize in the factory; if you are in school, evangelize at school; whether in a subway car or anywhere, evangelize. Even in gambling houses, do it.

When you go out to evangelize, those with a purpose will already sense it. In the past, when you went out to evangelize, didn’t you engage in a movement to find people? Back then, how hard did you work to find one person? Now, you can tell at a glance. From now on, those who cannot evangelize one person a month will absolutely not be allowed to come here. Some may say they cannot do it because they are responsible for their company. However, the teacher does not recognize that. The department heads here are no exception. Everyone must take responsibility. This pastor must also do it. Even if you are sitting here preaching, you must find time to do it.

Since I have commanded worldwide to evangelize one person a month, we will calculate what percentage Korea achieves. Then, in the future, each region will compete, and we will see what percentage each region achieves. The more people there are, the harder it will be. We will give scores for this and compile statistics, but the more people there are, the harder it will be. It is simple to go from 10 to 40 people. In a year, 40 people will become 480, which is also easy. Therefore, we must set such standards.

From now on, the teacher's plan is to absolutely not create large churches. If you create a church that can hold more than 120 people, it will become corrupt. That is for sure. Until now, there has been much persecution, so we had to support each other, but that is no longer the case. Now, the foundation is established for each person to follow their own will, so they must establish their own lifestyle and create a familial boundary that can contribute to the world of heaven and solidify their familial foundation. Because of that mission, blessed families must all do this from now on. Will you evangelize one person a month or not? "We will." Raise your hands if you will. If you will not, please leave. However, this is not to force you.

Let’s evangelize starting from those close to us. The teacher has made a total factory and has eaten a lot of insults. This time when I went to Japan, the Japanese government was in turmoil. Every time I go in and out, I cause an incident, so they are very interested. I thought they wouldn’t hold a joint wedding this time, but the teacher went ahead and did it. So they say, "Oh, that man causes an incident every time he comes."

Knowing this, from the beginning of June, one person must evangelize one person each month. Absolutely do not do two. Just because you managed to bring two people in the first month does not mean you can count one for the next month. That is like giving birth to twins. Therefore, you must evangelize one new person each month.

If you put in your heart for three people, one will surely come in. The time is right for that. Knowing this, please plan for all twelve months of the year. For each month, designate a first candidate, a second candidate, and a third candidate, including your parents, siblings, and everyone. If it’s a younger sibling, you can say, "Hey, let’s go." There is no need to show any understanding. If you cannot persuade them gently, you should drag them along even if you have to force them.
Evangelizing younger sisters or younger brothers is easy. Even if older brothers and sisters can't do it that way, they can forcibly bring their siblings along. There is a history where Cain, the elder brother, killed his younger brother Abel. Do you want to die at my hands? You must listen to your brother. By doing this, all younger sisters and younger brothers will easily come into the Unification Church. When you eat three meals a day, you should shed tears and pray about this. You should pray that your family, who cannot shed tears together for a common ideal while eating the same meal, can now praise the Father together and become those who can all worry about this country. Now, instead of trying to evangelize people far away, you should start by evangelizing close relatives and reach out to distant relatives as well. Do you understand? This is a gift I brought back from my recent trip abroad. I wanted to bring back a good gift, but since the Gimpo customs were trying to catch me on even the smallest thing, I couldn't do that. If someone from the Unification Church got caught smuggling something on their way back from abroad and it made the news, what would happen to the reputation of the Unification Church? So this time, I thought I would come back empty-handed. However, it would be disappointing to come back just like that. So, I went to the Dead Sea to collect stones to give to the department heads. This will probably become the most memorable good souvenir from the second tour. When I left Japan, I told the Japanese people that there couldn't be a better gift than this, and they were very pleased. I couldn't bring back many of these. 

This is a picture postcard. Since it would be a burden to bring them from far away, I bought all of them in Japan and brought back 600 pieces. I wanted to bring back a bit more, but if I brought too many, they would lose their value. It’s more interesting and valuable if there are some who cannot have them. The reason the teacher called you all together tonight is that there are 270 pieces left, and I want to share them with you. There may be more than 270 people here. I don't know if it exceeds that number. I will start distributing from the front, so the last person can figure out how to get theirs, whether by fighting or whatever. Who asked for the last person to come out? (Laughter) 

This will remain in history. This is worth 20 yen in Japanese money. It’s only worth 20 yen, but in a hundred years, or even in a few decades, this one piece will become an invaluable heirloom for your family, one that you can't buy for millions of won. So, I thought this would be the most suitable memento to give rather than anything else, and I’m distributing one to each of you. If you don’t want it, you don’t have to take it. (Laughter) It may take some time, but I will personally distribute them. 

<Prayer> We thank you for protecting us until this day. Please remember all our lives and guide us according to your will. We earnestly hope and wish that your abundant love may forever be with the homes of your beloved children and the young children born in those homes. 

Responsibilities of Korean Family Members  
Tomorrow, we will leave this place and visit eight regions. Starting from the first day of June, we have the responsibility and mission to unfold a new history, so please allow us to make this a time to promise ourselves before the Father that we will go forward with new resolutions and new determination. We know that we are in a destiny where we cannot rest before the suffering nation and the suffering humanity. We are bodies that have sworn before the Father, so we must not linger but pour out all our sincerity. We believe that when we dedicate ourselves for three years, the path of this country will become clear, so please help us to give our utmost sincerity. Rather than looking up high, let us go down low and walk the path, Father, please guide us. I ask that you personally oversee this period, and I pray all these things in the name of True Parents. Amen.
